# 产物目录

本文从“看到一个文件后怎么理解它”的角度列出关键 artifact。`docs/system_flow.md` 仍是工程事实源；本文是阅读索引，帮助使用者判断 artifact 的生成者、上游输入、下游用途、production 影响和常见误解。

如果需要理解输入数据如何计算成输出数据，先读 `docs/calculation_logic.md`；字段级含义见 `docs/schema/fields.yaml`，也可以用 `aits explain <field|gate|artifact>` 做只读反查。该 YAML 先覆盖 `scores_daily.csv`、decision snapshot、trace bundle、prediction ledger 和 shadow parameter search 的核心字段。

## ETF Portfolio runtime artifact policy

`data/etf_portfolio/`、`data/simulation/` 和 `reports/` 是本地运行产物目录，默认由 ETF daily run、simulation、backtest、P1/P2 observe-only reports 或 report integration 命令生成，并通过 `.gitignore` 排除在源码提交之外。它们可以作为本机审计证据和人工复核输入，但不是 source artifacts。

ETF deterministic test fixtures 只能提交到 `tests/fixtures/etf_portfolio/`。不要把测试 fixture 放进 `data/` 或 `reports/`，也不要把 daily run 生成的 report 复制成源码 fixture，除非另行建立明确的最小化、脱敏、确定性 fixture。

`config/report_registry.yaml` 中的 report entry 默认按 as-of 选择 artifact。显式标记 `artifact_selection_policy=latest_available` 的 ad-hoc research entry 只用于 Reader Brief/report index 的 latest 研究下钻，例如 Dynamic v3 parameter sweep leaderboard；这类记录会在 report index JSON/HTML 中披露 `artifact_temporal_relation=AFTER_AS_OF` 和 `artifact_after_as_of=true`，表示它是最新研究 evidence，不是 daily decision snapshot 的历史输入，也不允许补跑上游或生成 production action。

`config/report_index_visibility_waivers.yaml` 是 TRADING-352A/TRADING-375 report index visibility waiver source policy。该文件按 `waiver_id`、affected report registry entry / artifact family、`issue_status`、`report_id(s)`、owner、reason、accepted impact、validation coverage、exit condition、`created_at`、`expires_at`、`review_status` 和 `linked_task_id` 记录 legacy / optional missing 或 stale artifact exception；waiver 默认不能永久存在。`aits reports index` 只会把 `approved_active` 且未过期的 optional issue 写入 JSON 的 `explicit_waivers` 和每个 report 的 `visibility_waiver`，并在全部 warning 都有当前有效显式 waiver 时返回 `PASS_WITH_EXPLICIT_WAIVERS`。Expired 或 inactive waiver 不改变 artifact 的 `freshness_status`，不补造 report，不运行上游，也不能 waiver required daily missing 或 production-effect risk；`aits reports waiver-inventory` / `validate-waiver-inventory` 会 fail closed 暴露过期或缺 registry entry 的 waiver。

TRADING-421 exact blocker/warning inventory 是只读恢复治理 artifact，位于 `outputs/reports/exact_blocker_warning_inventory_YYYY-MM-DD.json/md` 和 `exact_blocker_warning_inventory_validation_YYYY-MM-DD.json/md`。`aits reports exact-blocker-warning-inventory --as-of YYYY-MM-DD` 读取 recovery blocker triage、post-recovery governance pack、source depth audit、report-index warning triage、normal paper-shadow observation clock 和 recovery owner action map，逐条输出当前 post-recovery source counts 下的 blocker、recovery warning 和 report-index unwaived warning 的 source artifact、upstream dependency、repair type、waiver eligibility、next action、normal/extended/live boundary 与 Reader Brief section。该 report 不运行上游、不刷新数据、不补造 signal/snapshot/metrics、不创建 waiver、不写 owner decision、不修改 paper-shadow/production state、不触发 broker/order；存在 blocker 时只把 `EXACT_INVENTORY_BLOCKED` 暴露给 owner review。

TRADING-429～438 decision-stage review 是只读 owner-decision 前置治理 artifact family，位于 `outputs/reports/eight_blocker_decision_review_YYYY-MM-DD.json/md`、`normal_shadow_gate_gap_analysis_YYYY-MM-DD.json/md`、`promotion_blocker_after_metrics_review_YYYY-MM-DD.json/md`、`candidate_research_return_assessment_YYYY-MM-DD.json/md`、`owner_decision_options_packet_YYYY-MM-DD.json/md`、`owner_decision_dry_run_YYYY-MM-DD.json/md`、`observation_clock_readiness_plan_YYYY-MM-DD.json/md`、`post_decision_rerun_plan_YYYY-MM-DD.json/md`、`report_quality_warning_drilldown_YYYY-MM-DD.json/md`、`governance_status_snapshot_after_decision_review_YYYY-MM-DD.json/md` 和 `eight_blocker_decision_review_validation_YYYY-MM-DD.json/md`。`aits reports decision-stage-review --as-of YYYY-MM-DD` 读取 current report index、research governance recovery pack、report quality gate、owner audit log 和 recovery pack source artifacts；`owner_decision_dry_run` 只验证 proposed record shape，必须保持 `would_append=false` / `real_entry_written=false`。这些 artifacts 不 append owner decision、不生成 signoff、不启动 observation clock、不恢复 normal shadow、不批准 extended shadow/live trading、不写 official target weights、不修改 candidate/paper-shadow/production state、不触发 broker/order。

TRADING-439～448 return-to-research reset 是 decision-stage 后的 research reset artifact family。`aits reports return-to-research-reset --as-of YYYY-MM-DD` 会记录显式 owner `return_to_research` decision（append-only JSONL；同 decision id 已存在时复用），并生成 `owner_return_to_research_decision_record`、`candidate_return_to_research_transition_pack`、`candidate_failure_mode_attribution`、`reusable_evidence_extraction`、`return_to_research_hypothesis_backlog`、`next_candidate_spec_draft`、`research_backfill_plan_for_next_candidate`、`archived_candidate_status_update`、`research_cycle_reset_pack`、`return_to_research_governance_snapshot` 和 `return_to_research_governance_snapshot_validation`。这些 artifacts 把 candidate 状态置为可审计的 `RETURNED_TO_RESEARCH`，但不 reject、不恢复 normal shadow、不批准 extended/live、不写 official target weights、不修改 production 或 broker/order。

TRADING-449～459 next research cycle 是 return-to-research 之后的 research-only artifact family。`aits reports next-research-cycle-intake`、`next-candidate-spec-freeze`、`next-candidate-backfill`、`next-candidate-stress-review`、`next-candidate-cost-benchmark-review`、`next-candidate-vs-returned-candidate-comparison`、`next-candidate-signal-robustness-review`、`next-candidate-overfit-window-sensitivity`、`next-candidate-research-gate`、`next-candidate-owner-research-review-packet` 和 `next-candidate-research-cycle-snapshot` 依次生成 `next_research_cycle_intake`、`next_candidate_spec_frozen`、`next_candidate_backfill`、`next_candidate_stress_review`、`next_candidate_cost_benchmark_review`、`next_candidate_vs_returned_candidate_comparison`、`next_candidate_signal_robustness_review`、`next_candidate_overfit_window_sensitivity`、`next_candidate_research_gate`、`next_candidate_owner_research_review_packet` 和 `next_candidate_research_cycle_snapshot`；对应 `validate-next-*` 命令可生成 validation artifacts，其中 final snapshot validation 为 `next_candidate_research_cycle_snapshot_validation`。这些 artifacts 不创建 paper-shadow candidate、不恢复 normal shadow、不批准 extended/live、不写 official target weights、不触发 broker/order、不 append owner decision、不修改 production；TRADING-451 在解释 backfill 前运行同一 validate-data code path，并在缺 executable next-candidate signal/weight binding 时 fail closed 为 more-evidence 状态。

TRADING-460 executable binding contract 是 TRADING-449～459 之后的 contract-only research artifact。`aits reports next-candidate-executable-binding-contract --as-of YYYY-MM-DD` 读取 frozen spec、final next research-cycle snapshot、backfill plan 和 research gate output，生成 `next_candidate_executable_binding_contract`；`aits reports validate-next-candidate-executable-binding-contract --latest` 生成 `next_candidate_executable_binding_contract_validation`。该 contract 只定义 required signal/feature inputs、allowed research-only state outputs、allowed hypothetical allocation output schema 和 forbidden outputs，不实现 signal behavior、不产生 hypothetical weights、不创建 paper-shadow、不写 official target weights、不触发 broker/order、不修改 production。

TRADING-461 executable signal binding 是 contract 后的 research-only signal state layer。`aits reports next-candidate-signal-binding --as-of YYYY-MM-DD` 先运行同一路径的 cached-data quality gate，然后读取 contract validation、frozen spec、signal input completeness policy、ETF signal series 和 feature matrix，生成 `next_candidate_signal_binding`；`aits reports validate-next-candidate-signal-binding --latest` 生成 validation。该 layer 只输出 candidate signal series、latest signal state、confidence/uncertainty 和 blocking reason；不输出 hypothetical research weights、official target weights、paper-shadow activation、broker/order、owner decision 或 backfill metrics。

TRADING-462 executable research weight binding 是 signal binding 后的 hypothetical-only allocation layer。`aits reports next-candidate-research-weight-binding --as-of YYYY-MM-DD` 先运行同一路径的 cached-data quality gate，然后读取 `next_candidate_signal_binding` 和 validation，按 governed research weight policy 输出 `next_candidate_research_weight_binding`；`aits reports validate-next-candidate-research-weight-binding --latest` 生成 validation。该 layer 只输出 hypothetical research weights、previous hypothetical weights、rotation delta、turnover proxy、risk state、constraint hits 和 blocking reason；不输出 official target weights、paper-shadow activation、broker/order、owner decision、production mutation 或 backfill return/drawdown/cost/benchmark metrics。

TRADING-463 executable binding safety audit 是 TRADING-464 backfill 前的 hard-stop safety gate。`aits reports executable-binding-safety-audit --as-of YYYY-MM-DD` 读取 signal binding、research weight binding 及其 validation artifacts，并扫描 binding module、research policy 和生成 artifacts 是否出现 official target weights、broker/order、live allocation、production mutation、account/API key、paper-shadow activation 或 owner decision append 语义；`aits reports validate-executable-binding-safety-audit --latest` 生成 validation。只有 `EXECUTABLE_BINDING_SAFETY_PASS` 或 acceptable `EXECUTABLE_BINDING_SAFETY_WARNING` 才允许继续 rerun backfill；`EXECUTABLE_BINDING_SAFETY_BLOCKED` 必须停止。

TRADING-464 binding-backed next candidate backfill 在 safety audit pass/acceptable warning 后运行。`aits reports next-candidate-backfill --as-of YYYY-MM-DD` 先运行同一路径的 validate-data quality gate，然后读取 executable signal binding、research-only weight binding、safety audit、frozen spec、backfill windows 和价格 cache，输出真实 return/drawdown/turnover/rotation/false-risk-off/constraint/signal-completeness proxy metrics；`aits reports validate-next-candidate-backfill --latest` 生成 validation。当前 binding 只有单点 signal/weight row 时，artifact 必须标为 `CANDIDATE_BACKFILL_PARTIAL` 和 static research-weight proxy，不得声明完整动态策略 backfill。

TRADING-465 stress/cost/benchmark rerun 使用 TRADING-464 的 complete 或 partial real metrics 重新生成 `next_candidate_stress_review`、`next_candidate_stress_review_validation`、`next_candidate_cost_benchmark_review` 和 `next_candidate_cost_benchmark_review_validation`。`aits reports next-candidate-stress-review --as-of YYYY-MM-DD` 从 backfill window metrics 输出 stress result、major blockers/warnings、worst return/drawdown proxy 和 scenario rows；`aits reports next-candidate-cost-benchmark-review --as-of YYYY-MM-DD` 用 aggregate return proxy 和 turnover proxy 计算 cost drag、net proxy、cost survival 和 candidate-vs-baseline delta。2026-06-17 真实 run 基于 `CANDIDATE_BACKFILL_PARTIAL` static proxy，stress 为 `WEAK`，cost/benchmark 为 `COST_BENCHMARK_REVIEW_WEAK`，validation 均 PASS；这些 artifacts 只支持继续 research comparison，不优化候选、不创建 paper-shadow、不写 official target weights、不触发 broker/order、不 append owner decision、不修改 production。

TRADING-466 vs-returned comparison 使用 returned candidate failure attribution、reusable/invalidated evidence、TRADING-464 real backfill、TRADING-465 stress review 和 TRADING-465 cost/benchmark review 生成 `next_candidate_vs_returned_candidate_comparison` 与 validation artifact。Comparison rows 覆盖 drawdown mismatch、flip/rotation、turnover、cost survival、benchmark-relative behavior、signal robustness 和 governance blockers，并明确标记 repeated failure mode。2026-06-17 真实 run 输出 `MIXED_VS_RETURNED_CANDIDATE`，benchmark relative behavior 为 `REPEATS_FAILURE_MODE`，drawdown mismatch 为 `REGRESSED_VS_REUSABLE_EVIDENCE`，validation PASS；该 artifact 不声明 improved、不进入 paper-shadow、不写 official target weights、不触发 broker/order、不 append owner decision、不修改 production。

TRADING-467 signal/window rerun 使用 executable signal binding 和 TRADING-464 real backfill window metrics 生成 `next_candidate_signal_robustness_review`、`next_candidate_signal_robustness_review_validation`、`next_candidate_overfit_window_sensitivity` 和 `next_candidate_overfit_window_sensitivity_validation` artifacts。Signal review 对 missing feature columns、partial signal series、stale signal series、schema mismatch 和 market coverage gap fail closed；window review 对 early/middle/recent/stress-heavy/calm diagnostic splits 输出 real split metrics、fragility、overfit risk 和 blocking conditions。2026-06-17 真实 run 输出 `SIGNAL_ROBUSTNESS_BLOCKED`（blocking checks=3）与 `WINDOW_FRAGILE`（`overfit_risk=HIGH`、weak splits=2、partial static proxy splits=3），validations PASS；该 artifact 不推进 paper-shadow、不写 official target weights、不触发 broker/order、不 append owner decision、不修改 production。

TRADING-468 research gate rerun 使用 executable binding safety audit、TRADING-464 real backfill、TRADING-465 stress/cost/benchmark reviews、TRADING-466 vs-returned comparison 和 TRADING-467 signal/window reviews 生成 `next_candidate_research_gate` 与 validation artifact。Gate taxonomy 限定为 `RESEARCH_PROMISING|NEEDS_MORE_EVIDENCE|RETURN_TO_HYPOTHESIS_BACKLOG|REJECT_RESEARCH_CANDIDATE`，并必须披露 strongest positive/negative evidence、blockers 和 required next action。2026-06-17 真实 run 输出 `NEEDS_MORE_EVIDENCE`，blockers=5，validation PASS；该 gate 不激活 paper-shadow、不写 official target weights、不触发 broker/order、不 append owner decision、不修改 production。

TRADING-075 data quality governance policy 是 source configuration，位于 `config/etf_portfolio/data_quality.yaml`。该文件定义 required / optional assets、price freshness lag、explicit market holiday baseline、calendar coverage lookback、missing bar limits、return outlier thresholds、corporate-action sanity、config/model drift report set、evidence completeness rules、validation gate freshness、report staleness、Reader Brief link checks 和固定 `observe_only=true`、`candidate_only=true`、`production_effect=none`、`broker_action=none`、`manual_review_required=true`。`aits etf data-quality report --as-of YYYY-MM-DD` 只读读取 price cache、当前 ETF config hash/model version、report registry 和既有 artifacts，生成 `reports/etf_portfolio/data_quality/governance/data_quality_report_YYYY-MM-DD.json/md`；report 暴露 `etf_data_quality_report_v1` schema、safety banner、run metadata、price freshness、calendar coverage/missing bars、return outliers/corporate-action sanity、config/model drift、evidence completeness、validation gate freshness、report staleness、Reader Brief links、blocking failures、warnings、manual review items 和 source links。Critical required data/artifact/gate/link failures 用于阻断 dependent research interpretation；optional missing artifacts 只 warning；report 不运行上游命令、不写 production weights、不触发 broker。`aits etf data-quality validate` 生成 `reports/etf_portfolio/data_quality/validation/data_quality_validation_YYYY-MM-DD.json/md`，使用 deterministic probes 校验 policy、checker availability、report generator、Reader Brief/report registry integration 和 safety boundary，固定 `commands_executed=false`、`production_state_mutated=false`。Reader Brief 的 `ETF Data Quality` 区块只读 latest governance report，展示 overall status、blockers、warnings、section status、detail link 和 safety posture；缺失时只显示 `MISSING`，不得补跑 data-quality CLI 或补造质量结论。

TRADING-076 strategy evidence dashboard registry 是 source configuration，位于 `config/etf_portfolio/evidence_dashboard.yaml`。该文件把 ETF baseline、weight calibration、forward simulation、AI confirmation / attribution、satellite replacement / attribution、parameter review、weekly review、decision journal、data quality、operations health 和 validation gates 映射到 evidence categories、freshness requirements、quality requirements、manual-review priority rules 和固定安全边界。`aits etf evidence-dashboard aggregate --as-of YYYY-MM-DD` 只读 report index 和 registry，生成 aggregation JSON；当 latest artifact 是 Markdown / HTML 且同名 JSON sidecar 存在时，aggregation 会读取 sidecar payload 的内部 `status` / `overall_status` 等状态，防止 blocked report 被误读为 artifact available。`aits etf evidence-dashboard report --as-of YYYY-MM-DD` 生成统一 strategy evidence dashboard JSON / Markdown；`aits etf evidence-dashboard validate --as-of YYYY-MM-DD` 生成 final validation gate。每个 evidence card 必须保留 source module、source report path、source metric、as-of date、freshness、data quality、validation status 和 sample count；缺失、stale、blocked 和 optional missing evidence 不得被隐藏或补造。所有输出固定 `observe_only=true`、`candidate_only=true`、`production_effect=none`、`broker_action=none`、`manual_review_required=true`、`commands_executed=false`、`production_state_mutated=false`。

TRADING-077 baseline review policy 是 source configuration，位于 `config/etf_portfolio/baseline_review.yaml`。该文件定义 ETF allocation candidate 进入 owner baseline review 前的 eligibility thresholds、required evidence matrix、blocking conditions、review checklist、decision capture policy、proposal draft policy、outcome tracking policy 和固定安全边界。`aits etf baseline-review eligibility/matrix/package --candidate <id>` 只读 report index、strategy evidence dashboard 和既有 ETF artifacts，生成 candidate review readiness、evidence matrix 和 manual review package；当 latest artifact path 指向 Markdown / HTML wrapper 时读取同名 JSON sidecar，weight calibration proposal action type 只作为证据状态归一，不作为 unsupported candidate type；`capture-decision` 只捕获人工决定并可链接 decision journal；`proposal-draft` 仅在 explicit owner approval 和 journal link 后生成 proposal-only draft；`outcome` 追踪 review cycle 状态；`validate` 是 TRADING-077 final safety gate。所有 baseline review artifacts 都固定 `observe_only=true`、`candidate_only=true`、`production_effect=none`、`broker_action=none`、`manual_review_required=true`，且 `production_state_mutated=false` / `baseline_config_mutated=false`；这些 artifacts 不能被解读为 baseline change、production promotion 或 broker action。

TRADING-080 weight calibration cache policy 是 source configuration，位于 `config/etf_portfolio/cache_policy.yaml`。该文件定义 diagnostics cache root、enabled layers、allowed cache modes、TTL、schema versions、parallel worker bounds、locking/pruning policy 和固定 safety boundary。`aits etf weight-calibration diagnostics --cache read-write/read-only --no-cache --force-refresh --workers auto --resume --run-id <run_id> --include-performance-report` 先通过 ETF price quality gate，再按 deterministic cache key 读取或写入 price/returns matrix、candidate backtest、regime robustness 和 diagnostics aggregation cache；cache entry manifest 校验 schema、safety、source config hash、data hash 和 engine version。Cache miss 的 per-candidate backtest / robustness 计算可通过 worker pool 并行执行，worker 只返回 validated payload，由 coordinator 写入 cache；cache-hit resume 会用指定 run id 写入新的 run manifest。Runtime cache 位于 ignored `data/cache/weight_calibration/`；run manifest 位于同一 cache root 的 `runs/<run_id>/run_manifest.json`；performance report 输出到 `reports/etf_portfolio/weight_calibration/performance/`。`aits etf weight-calibration performance-validate` 生成 cache / parallel validation gate，fail closed 校验 cache policy、key/manifest、price/returns payload、candidate/regime/aggregation cache behavior、parallel runner、resume manifest、performance report 和 safety boundary。TRADING-080 artifacts 只提高 repeatability 和 diagnostics runtime visibility，不注册 candidate、不 enroll shadow、不修改 production weights、不触发 broker。

TRADING-081 weight calibration profiling policy 是 source configuration，位于 `config/etf_portfolio/profiling_policy.yaml`。该文件定义 profiling modes、default mode、step/candidate/cache/worker/cProfile timing visibility、slow-step/candidate/cache thresholds、top-N 和固定 safety boundary。`aits etf weight-calibration diagnostics --profile off/summary/detailed/cprofile --profile-output <path> --profile-top-n N` 在既有 diagnostics 输出旁路记录 profiling metadata；默认 `summary` 是低开销 step/cache/worker timing，`detailed` 才展开 candidate hotspot table，`cprofile` 才生成 function-level stats。Runtime profiling artifacts 默认写入 ignored `reports/etf_portfolio/weight_calibration/profiling/<run_id>/`，包括 `profiling_report.json/md`、`candidate_hotspots.json/csv/md` 和 optional `cprofile.stats` / top functions JSON/Markdown。`aits etf weight-calibration profiling-validate` 生成 fail-closed safety gate，校验 policy、runtime profiler、hotspot/report builders、Reader Brief/report registry integration 和 safety boundary。TRADING-081 artifacts 只回答 cold run 时间分布和后续优化建议，不改变 diagnostics ranking、candidate readiness、shadow enrollment、production weights、baseline config 或 broker state，也不引入 native / Numba / Polars rewrite。

TRADING-082 shadow-ready review policy 是 source configuration，位于 `config/etf_portfolio/shadow_ready_review.yaml`。该文件定义 review thresholds、ranking weights、hard blockers、owner approval policy、enrollment limits、review checklist 和固定 safety boundary。`aits etf shadow-review package --latest --top N` 只读 TRADING-079 diagnostics JSON、stable shapes CSV 和 near-shadow CSV，按 weight_shape 聚合 `shadow_ready` observations，输出 ranked stable shapes、near-shadow context、owner checklist、decision options 和 source links；`approve` 只捕获 owner decision；`enroll-approved` 只有在 `approved_for_shadow` approval 存在时才生成 forward tracking link；`validate` 是 TRADING-082 final gate。所有 artifacts 固定 `observe_only=true`、`candidate_only=true`、`production_effect=none`、`broker_action=none`、`manual_review_required=true`、`commands_executed=false`、`production_state_mutated=false`；它们不能被解读为 production baseline replacement、automatic promotion、broker action 或 auto-enrollment without approval。

TRADING-083 trend signal calibration policy 是 source configuration，位于 `config/etf_portfolio/trend_calibration.yaml`。该文件定义 two-layer dynamic ETF allocation roadmap 的 Layer 1 signal registry、bounded preset signal weights、score bands、forward attribution windows、redundancy diagnostics、regime stability review 和固定 safety boundary。`aits etf trend-calibration run --start YYYY-MM-DD --end YYYY-MM-DD` 在生成 dataset / report 前先运行 `aits validate-data` 等价 cached market / macro data quality gate，随后只读 ETF price / feature inputs，输出 evaluation-only trend signal dataset、candidate-only score config registry 和 calibration report；`report --latest` 只读 latest report；`validate` 是 TRADING-083 final gate。所有 forward return / drawdown fields 固定 `evaluation_only=true`，所有 artifacts 固定 `observe_only=true`、`candidate_only=true`、`production_effect=none`、`broker_action=none`、`manual_review_required=true`；它们不能被解读为 ETF target weights、baseline config mutation、production weight update、broker order 或 automatic candidate promotion。

TRADING-084 dynamic allocation policy 是 source configuration，位于 `config/etf_portfolio/dynamic_allocation_policy.yaml`。该文件定义 two-layer dynamic ETF allocation roadmap 的 Layer 2 base weights、regime weight targets、trend overlays、event-risk cash overlay、exposure constraints、rebalance gates 和固定 safety boundary。`aits etf dynamic-allocation decide --date YYYY-MM-DD --score-profile ...` 只生成 candidate-only dynamic allocation decision record、policy registry 和 report；`report --latest` 只读 latest report；`validate` 是 TRADING-084 final gate。TRADING-084 可以输出 `candidate_target_weights` 作为人工复核对象，但固定 `production_effect=none`、`broker_action=none`、`production_state_mutated=false`、`baseline_config_mutated=false`、`official_target_weights_mutated=false`；它们不能被解读为 official `data/etf_portfolio/target_weights.csv` write、baseline replacement、production weight update、broker order 或 automatic candidate promotion。

TRADING-085 dynamic calibration policy 是 source configuration，位于 `config/etf_portfolio/dynamic_calibration.yaml`。该文件定义 two-layer candidate pack schema、two-stage search protocol metadata、coarse-to-fine iteration、trend score / allocation path / dynamic calibration proxy cache layers、parallel worker policy、ranking weights 和固定 safety boundary。`aits etf dynamic-calibration run --pack ... --cache ... --workers ...` 只生成 candidate pack collection 和 batch report；`report --latest` 只读 latest report；`validate` 是 TRADING-085 final gate。TRADING-085 的 `dynamic_backtest` cache 是 calibration proxy，用于准备 TRADING-086 robustness review 输入，不是完整 walk-forward / false-signal backtest 结论；所有输出固定 `production_effect=none`、`broker_action=none`、`official_target_weights_mutated=false`、`automatic_candidate_promotion=false`、`auto_enrollment_without_owner_approval=false`。

TRADING-087 dynamic shadow policy 是 source configuration，位于 `config/etf_portfolio/dynamic_shadow.yaml`。该文件定义 dynamic shadow required gates、owner approval decisions、approved-only enrollment limits、forward tracking metrics、weekly review statuses / thresholds 和固定 safety boundary。`aits etf dynamic-shadow package/approve/enroll-approved/update/weekly-review/validate` 只生成 owner review、approval、forward observation 和 validation artifacts；`update` 使用 cached price data 时必须先通过 `aits validate-data` 等价门禁。所有输出固定 `production_effect=none`、`broker_action=none`、`official_target_weights_mutated=false`、`automatic_candidate_promotion=false`、`auto_enrollment_without_owner_approval=false`；owner-approved forward shadow observation 不代表 production approval。

TRADING-088 dynamic failure diagnostics policy 是 source configuration，位于 `config/etf_portfolio/dynamic_failure_diagnostics.yaml`。该文件定义 failed dynamic v0.1 classification thresholds、false risk-off/on definitions、signal buckets、turnover/constraint thresholds、bounded rescue templates、improvement requirements 和固定 safety boundary。`aits etf dynamic-rescue run --base-candidate <candidate_id>` 或 `--latest-failed-package` 会先通过 `aits validate-data` 等价门禁，再只读读取 failed dynamic robustness / optional dynamic shadow package evidence，生成 failure diagnostics dataset、Layer 1/Layer 2 attribution、false signal attribution、turnover/constraint breakdown、v0.2-v0.5 rescue candidate comparison 和 evaluation report；`report --latest` 只读 latest report；`validate` 是 TRADING-088 final gate。所有输出固定 `production_effect=none`、`broker_action=none`、`official_target_weights_mutated=false`、`automatic_candidate_promotion=false`、`auto_enrollment_without_owner_approval=false`、`shadow_enrollment_allowed=false`、`automatic_enrollment_allowed=false`、`owner_approval_executed=false`；rescue candidate found 不代表 approval、shadow enrollment、baseline replacement、production weight update 或 broker action。

TRADING-089 Dynamic v0.2 review policy 是 source configuration，位于 `config/etf_portfolio/dynamic_v2_review.yaml`。该文件定义 `dynamic_regime_overlay_v0_4_lower_turnover` review thresholds、positive evidence thresholds、constraint/drawdown blockers、required regimes、benchmark set、review package policy 和固定 safety boundary。`aits etf dynamic-v2-review package --latest-rescue-report` 只读 TRADING-088 rescue evaluation、v0.4 candidate robustness report 和 optional dynamic shadow package，生成 review-only package；`report --latest` 只读 latest package；`validate` 是 TRADING-089 final gate。所有输出固定 `review_candidate / not_shadow_ready`、`shadow_enrollment_allowed=false`、`automatic_enrollment_allowed=false`、`owner_approval_executed=false`、`commands_executed=false`、`production_state_mutated=false`；positive evidence 不能抵消 constraint hit worsening 或 drawdown preservation failure，package 不代表 approval、shadow enrollment、baseline replacement、production weight update 或 broker action。

TRADING-090 Dynamic v0.3 constraint-aware rescue policy 是 source configuration，位于 `config/etf_portfolio/dynamic_v3_constraint_aware_rescue.yaml`。该文件定义 v0.4 blocker target、preservation target、drawdown target、pre-constraint normalization caps、soft constraint penalty、allocation smoothing、drawdown guardrail、emergency risk-off、v0.3a-v0.3d candidate templates、evaluation statuses 和固定 safety boundary。`aits etf dynamic-v3-rescue run --latest-v2-review` 只读 TRADING-089 v0.4 review package，生成 candidate-only v0.3 rescue evaluation report；`report --latest` 只读 latest report；`validate` 是 TRADING-090 final gate。所有输出固定 `review_candidate / not_shadow_ready`、`shadow_enrollment_allowed=false`、`automatic_enrollment_allowed=false`、`owner_approval_executed=false`、`commands_executed=false`、`production_state_mutated=false`；v0.3 rescue success 只表示可进入 owner review / TRADING-091 handoff，不代表 approval、shadow enrollment、baseline replacement、production weight update 或 broker action。

TRADING-091 Dynamic v0.3 rescue real evaluation policy 是 source configuration，位于 `config/etf_portfolio/dynamic_v3_real_evaluation.yaml`。该文件定义 v0.3a-v0.3d in-memory materialization controls、baseline/v0.2/v0.4/static/benchmark comparison set、promotion gate thresholds、overfit thresholds、Reader Brief section metadata 和固定 no-enrollment safety boundary。`aits etf dynamic-v3-rescue real-evaluate` 必须先执行 `aits validate-data` 等价 cached market / macro data quality gate，再复用 TRADING-086 price-driven robustness path 输出真实历史评估和 `promote_candidate` / `observe_only` / `reject` gate；`real-report --latest` 只读 latest report；`validate-real` 是 TRADING-091 validation gate。Gate label 只表示人工复核候选资格，不代表 automatic promotion、owner approval、shadow enrollment、baseline mutation、official target weight write、production mutation 或 broker action。

TRADING-092 Dynamic v0.3 rescue failure attribution policy 是 source configuration，位于 `config/etf_portfolio/dynamic_v3_failure_attribution.yaml`。该文件定义 latest TRADING-091 real evaluation reject input contract、constraint bucket concentration thresholds、v0.4 promotion-review thresholds、v0.5 design recommendation labels、Reader Brief section metadata 和固定 no-enrollment safety boundary。`aits etf dynamic-v3-rescue failure-attribution` 必须先执行 `aits validate-data` 等价 cached market / macro data quality gate，再从相同 source configs 和 cached ETF price data 重建 v0.3 / v0.4 robustness daily paths，用于输出 v0.3 rejection attribution、v0.3 vs v0.4 metric delta、constraint hit reason/regime/ticker/rebalance-window bucket、drawdown degradation attribution、overfit `REVIEW_REQUIRED` 原因解释、v0.4 promotion review 和 v0.5 design recommendation；`failure-attribution-report --latest` 只读 latest report；`validate-attribution` 是 TRADING-092 validation gate。Review / recommendation label 只表示人工复核优先级，不代表 automatic promotion、owner approval、shadow enrollment、baseline mutation、official target weight write、production mutation 或 broker action。

TRADING-074 operations schedule spec 是 source configuration，位于 `config/etf_portfolio/operations_schedule.yaml`。该文件定义 ETF portfolio research 的 daily / weekly / biweekly / monthly / manual-review steps、commands、dependencies、expected outputs、max_allowed_age、failure_policy 和 owner review requirement，并固定 `observe_only=true`、`candidate_only=true`、`production_effect=none`、`broker_action=none`、`manual_review_required=true`。`src/ai_trading_system/etf_portfolio/operations.py` 的 loader/validator 校验 schema、唯一 `step_id`、非空 command、依赖引用、required step expected outputs 和 unsafe safety fields；`build_daily_operations_command_graph`、`build_weekly_operations_command_graph`、`build_biweekly_operations_command_graph` 和 `build_monthly_operations_command_graph` 把对应 cadence schedule 转成 dry-run-only 内存 graph，暴露 node_id、command、inputs、outputs、dependencies、external_dependencies、required、failure_policy、estimated_runtime_class、owner_review_required 和 safety fields，且不执行命令、不写 artifact。Weekly / biweekly / monthly graph 把跨 cadence 上游保留为 `external_dependencies`，用于后续 freshness / blocking gate 审计；pilot config 可把 parameter review 节点标成 optional 后跳过。Monthly graph 把 bounded historical `weight_calibration_search` 标记为 `slow` runtime class，并确认它不进入 daily / weekly / biweekly graph。`check_operations_artifact_freshness` 是 TRADING-074E 只读 freshness / dependency checker，从 graph 和 schedule spec 生成 `etf_operations_artifact_freshness_v1` 内存报告；每个 artifact record 暴露 artifact_id、path、artifact_type、source_step、as_of_date、generated_at、max_allowed_age、required、freshness_status、dependency_status、dependency_steps、blocking_dependencies 和 age_days。它支持 JSON / text / filename date parsing、`{as_of}` 渲染、`{run_id}` 等动态占位符 glob resolution、required stale/missing/unknown blocking、optional missing warning 和 upstream blocking dependency propagation。`evaluate_operations_failure_policy` 是 TRADING-074F 只读 failure policy evaluator，从 freshness report 生成 `etf_operations_failure_policy_v1` 内存报告；每个 event 暴露 event_id、event_type、source_step、artifact_id、freshness_status、dependency_status、required、failure_policy、severity、blocks_pipeline、blocks_dependent_steps、requires_manual_review、blocking_dependencies 和 recommended_action，并输出 blocking / warning / manual-review event lists、severity summary 和 failure policy summary。它把 validation gate failure 评为 `critical` + `fail_pipeline`，optional missing artifact 评为 `warning` + `skip_optional_step`，required stale artifact 评为 `error` + `block_dependent_steps`，manual-review artifact failure 评为 `error` + `manual_review_required`。`build_operations_owner_review_checklist` 是 TRADING-074G 只读 owner checklist builder，从 `manual_review_steps` 和可选 failure policy report 生成 `etf_operations_owner_review_checklist_v1` 内存报告；report 暴露 cadence、checklist_step_id、checklist_command、dependencies、expected_outputs、checklist_status、source_pipeline_status、source_event_count、required_items、blocking_items、warning_items、manual_review_items 和 items，每个 item 暴露 item_id、category、required、blocking、owner_action、source_step、related_event_ids、related_artifact_ids 和 evidence_paths。它为 daily / weekly / monthly / incident owner review 固化 safety boundary、cadence gate、failure summary、blocking / warning / manual-review event 和 signoff。`build_operations_scheduler_dry_run` 和 `aits etf ops dry-run --cadence ... --as-of ...` 是 TRADING-074H 只读 scheduler simulation，从 graph、freshness report、failure policy report 和 owner checklist 生成 `etf_operations_scheduler_dry_run_v1` dry-run JSON；report 暴露 dry_run_id、cadence、as_of_date、status、planned_steps、execution_order、skipped_optional_steps、blocking_failures、warnings、expected_outputs、source schema versions、owner_checklist_status 和 safety，每个 planned step 暴露 command、dependencies、required、failure_policy、runtime class、expected_outputs、related_artifact_ids、blocking/warning/manual-review event ids、`command_would_execute=true` 和 `command_executed=false`。它可以写 ignored `outputs/dry_runs/etf_operations/` dry-run artifact，但不执行 planned commands、不写 production state、不替代 `config/scheduled_tasks.yaml` 的统一 daily scheduler trigger。`build_operations_health_report`、`write_operations_health_report` 和 `aits etf ops report --cadence ... --as-of ...` 是 TRADING-074I operations health report generator，从 source config、graph、freshness report、failure policy report、owner checklist 和 dry-run report 生成 `etf_operations_health_report_v1` JSON / Markdown；默认 runtime 输出位于 ignored `reports/etf_portfolio/operations/<cadence>/operations_health_<as_of>.json/md`。Report 暴露 report_id、cadence、as_of_date、status、safety_banner、run_metadata、pipeline_schedule、command_graph_summary、artifact_freshness_summary、dependency_status、failures、warnings、owner_review_checklist、expected_next_run、source_artifacts、source_schema_versions 和 source_dry_run_id，并固定 `commands_executed=false`、`production_state_mutated=false`。TRADING-074J Reader Brief `Operations Health` 区块只读 `config/report_registry.yaml` / report index 的 latest `etf_operations_health_report` artifact，展示 status、blocking failures、warnings、stale/missing artifacts、next owner review、safety posture 和 detail link；缺失时只显示 section-level `MISSING`，不运行上游、不补造状态。TRADING-074K `build_operations_validation_report` 和 `aits etf ops validate --as-of ...` 从该 source config、daily/weekly/biweekly/monthly graph、deterministic freshness probes、failure policy report、owner checklist、dry-run report、operations health report 和 Reader Brief registry integration 生成 `etf_operations_validation_v1` final gate，fail-closed 校验 workflow availability、required missing blocker、optional missing warning、unsafe safety fields 和 dependency cycle。

TRADING-064 controlled calibration experiment definitions 是 source configuration，位于 `config/etf_portfolio/experiments.yaml` 和 `config/etf_portfolio/experiment_packs.yaml`。这些文件只定义允许观察的 experiment registry、`etf_calibration_v1` pack、`risk_adjusted_v1` ranking policy、`shadow_only_manual_review` candidate gate policy、`weekly_shadow_review_v1` review policy 和安全边界，不是 runtime 结果；batch run 后的 `comparison_report.json/md` 和 `candidate_selection_report.json/md` 生成在 `reports/etf_portfolio/experiments/<run_id>/`，只能作为 shadow/manual-review 输入。`aits etf experiments enroll-shadow` 生成 `data/simulation/etf_shadow_candidates.json`，登记 `eligible_for_shadow` candidate 的 `shadow_id`、model/config hash、source run 和 evaluation schedule；`aits etf experiments weekly-review` 生成 `reports/etf_portfolio/experiments/weekly_reviews/weekly_review_YYYY-MM-DD.json/md`，只读比较 candidate/baseline/QQQ、drawdown、turnover、constraint hits 和 recommended action；`aits etf experiments validate --pack etf_calibration_v1` 生成 `reports/etf_portfolio/experiments/validation/*_experiment_validation.json/md`，作为 TRADING-064 final safety gate。上述文件都在 ignored runtime 目录，不是 source artifact，并保留 `observe_only=true`、`production_effect=none`、`broker_action=none`、`manual_review_required=true`、`production_promotion_allowed=false`。这些 runtime artifacts 已登记到 `config/report_registry.yaml`，由 `aits reports index` 和 Reader Brief 只读发现；缺失时只能显示 `MISSING`，不得补跑 experiment 或补造 candidate 状态。

TRADING-065 forward simulation policy 是 source configuration，位于 `config/etf_portfolio/forward_simulation.yaml`。该文件治理 rolling windows、candidate lifecycle thresholds、allowed statuses、allowed review/watchlist actions 和 safety boundary；它是 pilot baseline policy，不是 production allocation policy。`aits etf forward update --date YYYY-MM-DD` / `--latest` 只读取 shadow candidate registry、ETF price cache、baseline config 和 benchmarks，写入 evaluation-only update report、更新 shadow registry 的 evaluation metadata，并把 decision-time rows 追加到 `data/simulation/etf_forward_decisions.csv`；decision ledger 不得包含 `forward_*` 或其他 future/evaluation fields。`aits etf forward dashboard --latest`、`aits etf forward weekly-review --latest`、`aits etf forward watchlist --latest` 和 `aits etf forward validate` 分别生成 dashboard、weekly review、local watchlist 和 final validation gate。所有输出都在 ignored runtime 目录，固定 `observe_only=true`、`production_effect=none`、`broker_action=none`、`manual_review_required=true`、`production_promotion_allowed=false`，不得写 official target weights、替换 baseline 或触发 broker。Forward artifacts 已登记到 `config/report_registry.yaml`，daily ops 会在 report index 和 Reader Brief 之前刷新 update/dashboard/watchlist；Reader Brief 只读展示 `ETF Forward Simulation` 摘要。

TRADING-066 AI confirmation universe 是 source configuration，位于 `config/etf_portfolio/ai_confirmation_universe.yaml`。该文件定义 mega-cap AI、semiconductor hardware、cloud AI platform、AI ETF proxy 和 event-risk reference groups 的 ticker/name/group/role/enabled/weight_cap/benchmark/data_required/optional metadata，并固定 `observe_only=true`、`candidate_only=true`、`production_effect=none`、`broker_action=none`、`manual_review_required=true`。`config/etf_portfolio/ai_confirmation_policy.yaml` 治理 score bands、MegaCapAIScore component weights、AI semiconductor relative-strength pair definitions/weights、event risk severity/bands、relative-strength normalization、drawdown penalty、event-risk adjustment、composite weights、shadow overlay thresholds/constraints 和 coverage warning floor。`aits etf ai-confirmation features --date YYYY-MM-DD` 生成 `reports/etf_portfolio/ai_confirmation/features/ai_confirmation_features_YYYY-MM-DD.json/csv`，只包含 price-derived breadth features、data coverage 和 warnings；运行前必须通过 ETF price quality gate，strict required universe data 缺失时 fail closed。`MegaCapAIScore`、`AISemiconductorRelativeStrengthScore`、event risk overlay 和 `AIConfirmationScore` composite 先作为 report 前的内存 payload，包含 score/risk value、band、component_scores or active/upcoming/recent events、drivers/reason codes、action_hint、coverage or pair features、policy version/hash 和 safety fields。`aits etf ai-confirmation report --date YYYY-MM-DD` 生成 `reports/etf_portfolio/ai_confirmation/reports/ai_confirmation_report_YYYY-MM-DD.json/md`，汇总 safety banner、AIConfirmationScore、component score table、semiconductor breadth、mega-cap AI confirmation、AI/semiconductor relative strength、event risk、data coverage、top drivers、candidate-only usage note 和 shadow experiment usage note；该 report 已登记到 `config/report_registry.yaml`，由 `aits reports index` 只读发现。`aits etf ai-confirmation overlay --date YYYY-MM-DD --candidate <candidate_id>` 只读取显式 base candidate weights 和 AI confirmation report，输出 bounded candidate-only `after_candidate_weights`、`candidate_weights`、`shadow_weights` 和 `hypothetical_weights` 到 ignored overlay artifacts。它不产生 production target weights，也不替换 TRADING-064/065 的 shadow candidate 或 forward artifacts；后续 validation artifacts 必须从该 config/feature/report/overlay output 读取 universe membership、coverage 和 safety fields。

TRADING-072 AI confirmation forward attribution review 是 evaluation-only runtime artifact。`aits etf ai-attribution build --as-of YYYY-MM-DD` 只读 latest 或指定窗口内的 `ai_confirmation_report_*.json` 与 ETF price cache，先通过 ETF price quality gate，输出 `reports/etf_portfolio/ai_attribution/datasets/ai_attribution_dataset_YYYY-MM-DD.json/csv/md`。Dataset row 把 `score_date`、`forward_window`、`evaluation_as_of_date`、`evaluation_only=true`、AI/component scores、regime、QQQ/SPY/SMH/SOXX forward returns、SMH-QQQ / QQQ-SPY relative returns、forward drawdown/volatility、sample availability 和 source report path 串联起来；forward returns 只能用于 attribution/evaluation，不得进入 decision-time record。`aits etf ai-attribution report --as-of YYYY-MM-DD` 输出 `reports/etf_portfolio/ai_attribution/reports/ai_attribution_report_YYYY-MM-DD.json/md`，包含 bucket analysis、component attribution、regime attribution、event-risk attribution、redundancy diagnostics、evidence scorecard、manual review recommendation 和 source links。`aits etf ai-attribution validate` 输出 `reports/etf_portfolio/ai_attribution/validation/ai_attribution_validation_YYYY-MM-DD.json/md`，确认 workflow、Reader Brief/report registry visibility、evaluation-only separation、安全字段和 forbidden production/trading output keys。Reader Brief 的 `AI Attribution Review` 区块只读 latest report；缺失时只能显示 `MISSING`，不得补跑上游或补造 attribution 结论。所有 outputs 固定 `observe_only=true`、`candidate_only=true`、`production_effect=none`、`broker_action=none`、`manual_review_required=true`；常见误解是把 positive attribution 当成 production overlay approval，实际它只能降低或提高人工复核的证据强度，不能自动 promotion、不能改 baseline config、不能写 production weights。

TRADING-067 satellite stock replacement policy 是 source configuration + runtime artifact 组合。`config/etf_portfolio/satellite_universe.yaml` 定义 AI / semiconductor 个股、benchmark ETF、sleeve、role、optional flag、data coverage 和 event risk group；`config/etf_portfolio/satellite_policy.yaml` 治理 score bands、component weights、eligibility thresholds、single-name/sleeve/residual ETF/risk constraints、validation evidence 和 review condition。`aits etf satellite features --date YYYY-MM-DD` 生成 `reports/etf_portfolio/satellite/features/satellite_features_YYYY-MM-DD.json/csv`，只使用 `date <= score_date` 的 stock/benchmark ETF 价格计算 relative strength、trend、momentum、drawdown、volatility 和 coverage features。`aits etf satellite report --date YYYY-MM-DD` / `run` 生成 `reports/etf_portfolio/satellite/reports/satellite_replacement_report_YYYY-MM-DD.json/md`，包含 universe coverage、SatelliteCandidateScore、replacement eligibility gate、candidate/shadow/hypothetical replacement plan、risk constraint diagnostics、AI confirmation context 和 safety fields；`aits etf satellite experiment --date YYYY-MM-DD` 生成 ignored runtime shadow experiment；`aits etf satellite validate` 生成 `reports/etf_portfolio/satellite/validation/satellite_validation_YYYY-MM-DD.json/md`。这些 artifacts 已登记到 `config/report_registry.yaml`，Reader Brief 只读展示 `Satellite Replacement` 摘要。默认 ETF first；数据不足、gate fail 或风险约束触发时输出 `fallback_to_etf=true`，不得写 official ETF target weights、不得触发 broker action、不得自动 promotion。

TRADING-073 satellite replacement forward attribution review 是 evaluation-only runtime artifact。`aits etf satellite-attribution build --as-of YYYY-MM-DD` 只读 latest 或指定窗口内的 `satellite_replacement_report_*.json`、可选 `ai_confirmation_report_*.json` 与 ETF/satellite price cache，先通过 ETF price quality gate，输出 `reports/etf_portfolio/satellite_attribution/datasets/satellite_attribution_dataset_YYYY-MM-DD.json/csv/md`。Dataset row 把 `decision_date`、`eligibility_date`、`replacement_plan_date`、`forward_window`、`evaluation_as_of_date`、`evaluation_only=true`、ticker/benchmark/role/group、eligibility status、SatelliteCandidateScore/component scores、fallback flag、replacement weight、stock-vs-benchmark forward returns、replacement-vs-ETF impact、drawdown/volatility、event flag、sample availability 和 source report path 串联起来；forward returns 只能用于 attribution/evaluation，不得进入 decision-time record。`aits etf satellite-attribution report --as-of YYYY-MM-DD` 输出 `reports/etf_portfolio/satellite_attribution/reports/satellite_attribution_report_YYYY-MM-DD.json/md`，包含 eligibility bucket analysis、stock-vs-benchmark attribution、fallback-to-ETF attribution、score attribution、risk attribution、role/group attribution、AI interaction attribution、evidence scorecard、manual review recommendation 和 source links。`aits etf satellite-attribution validate` 输出 `reports/etf_portfolio/satellite_attribution/validation/satellite_attribution_validation_YYYY-MM-DD.json/md`，确认 workflow、Reader Brief/report registry visibility、evaluation-only separation、安全字段和 forbidden production/trading output keys。Reader Brief 的 `Satellite Attribution Review` 区块只读 latest report；缺失时只能显示 `MISSING`，不得补跑上游或补造 attribution 结论。所有 outputs 固定 `observe_only=true`、`candidate_only=true`、`production_effect=none`、`broker_action=none`、`manual_review_required=true`；常见误解是把 eligible stock positive attribution 当成 official ETF replacement approval，实际它只能支持人工复核，不能自动 promotion、不能改 baseline config、不能写 production weights。

TRADING-068 ETF weekly portfolio review 是 runtime 汇总报告，不新增 production allocation policy。`aits etf weekly-review aggregate --as-of YYYY-MM-DD` 只读扫描 `config/report_registry.yaml` / optional report index 指向的 ETF brief、target weights、experiment weekly review、forward dashboard/watchlist、AI confirmation、satellite replacement 和 validation gate artifacts，输出 `reports/etf_portfolio/weekly_review/aggregation/weekly_review_aggregation_YYYY-MM-DD.json`。`aits etf weekly-review generate --as-of YYYY-MM-DD` 生成 `reports/etf_portfolio/weekly_review/weekly_review_YYYY-MM-DD.json/md`，集中 portfolio decision summary、shadow candidate review、AI confirmation review、satellite replacement review、risk/watchlist/constraints、manual review action items、source report links、validation status 和 next-week watch items。`aits etf weekly-review validate` 生成 `reports/etf_portfolio/weekly_review/validation/weekly_review_validation_YYYY-MM-DD.json/md`，确认 report generator、Reader Brief integration、source traceability、unsafe action blocking 和 safety fields。所有 weekly review 输出固定 `observe_only=true`、`candidate_only=true`、`production_effect=none`、`broker_action=none`、`manual_review_required=true`；缺失可选 report 只能显示 `missing_data` / `REPORT_NOT_FOUND`，不得补跑上游、补造结论、写 official target weights 或触发 broker。

TRADING-069 ETF portfolio decision journal 是人工复核后的 runtime state + report。`aits etf decision-journal add/update/list/remove` 维护 ignored state `data/simulation/etf_portfolio_decision_journal.json`，每个 active entry 必须链接 TRADING-068 weekly review JSON 和 `manual_review_actions[].action_id`，并保留 source section、action snapshot、source evidence、rationale、confidence、follow-up task 和 audit trail。`remove` 只把 entry 移到 `removed_entries`，不静默删除。`aits etf decision-journal report --as-of YYYY-MM-DD` 生成 `reports/etf_portfolio/decision_journal/decision_journal_YYYY-MM-DD.json/md/html`，`analytics` 生成 review outcome JSON，`propose-state-updates` 只生成 candidate state proposal，`validate` 生成 `reports/etf_portfolio/decision_journal/validation/decision_journal_validation_YYYY-MM-DD.json/md`。所有 journal artifacts 固定 `observe_only=true`、`candidate_only=true`、`production_effect=none`、`broker_action=none`、`manual_review_required=true`；proposal 不修改 shadow registry、production weights 或 broker state。

TRADING-070 ETF allocation parameter review 聚合 forward evidence，不新增 production allocation policy。`aits etf parameter-review aggregate --as-of YYYY-MM-DD` 只读扫描 `config/report_registry.yaml` / optional report index 指向的 forward dashboard、forward weekly review、watchlist、TRADING-068 weekly review、TRADING-069 decision journal、experiment comparison、candidate selection 和 validation gates，输出 `reports/etf_portfolio/parameter_review/aggregation/parameter_review_evidence_YYYY-MM-DD.json/md`。Aggregation payload 保留 source report paths、candidate evidence records、metrics、journal/weekly links、validation status、missing source warnings 和 safety banner；缺少 forward dashboard 或 forward candidate rows 时输出 `needs_more_data` / `INSUFFICIENT_FORWARD_EVIDENCE`，缺失可选 source 不允许用补造结论解决。`aits etf parameter-review report --as-of YYYY-MM-DD` / `run` 生成 `reports/etf_portfolio/parameter_review/reports/parameter_review_YYYY-MM-DD.json/md`，把 evidence aggregation、candidate comparison、journal linkage、proposal package、governance scorecard、manual review requirements、next steps 和 source links 汇总为人工 review package。`aits etf parameter-review validate` 生成 `reports/etf_portfolio/parameter_review/validation/parameter_review_validation_YYYY-MM-DD.json/md`，确认 schema、aggregator、comparison、journal linker、proposal generator、governance gate、report generator、Reader Brief visibility、source links 和 unsafe action blocking。Reader Brief 的 `ETF Parameter Review` 区块只读 latest `etf_parameter_review_report`，展示 status、candidate/proposal counts、main reason、safety posture 和 detail link；缺失时显示 `MISSING`，不补跑上游。所有 parameter review artifacts 固定 `observe_only=true`、`candidate_only=true`、`production_effect=none`、`broker_action=none`、`manual_review_required=true`；当前阶段只建立 evidence/proposal package，不修改 baseline config、production weights、shadow registry 或 broker state。

TRADING-071 ETF allocation dual-track weight calibration 先建立 historical candidate search，不新增 production allocation policy。`config/etf_portfolio/weight_search.yaml` 是 source configuration，定义 `etf_initial_weight_search_v1` 的 universe、5% bounded grid、candidate cap、objective policy、benchmark set、walk-forward windows、regime split labels 和固定 safety boundary。TRADING-078A 新增 `config/etf_portfolio/weight_calibration_presets.yaml` source configuration，定义 `last_2y`、`last_3y`、`last_5y`、`post_2022_bear`、`ai_cycle_recent` 和 `full_available` historical range presets；每个 preset 记录 start policy、end-date policy、minimum required assets、coverage ratio、benchmark set、intended use 和固定 safety boundary。`aits etf weight-calibration search --search etf_initial_weight_search_v1 --preset <preset_id>` 先通过 ETF price quality gate，再把 preset 解析为实际 requested date range，并把 `historical_range_preset` 写入 search payload；不传 preset 时仍可显式传 `--start/--end`。Search 枚举有效 grid 并按 config 上限选择 deterministic bounded subset，生成 `reports/etf_portfolio/weight_calibration/<run_id>/summary.json/md`、`metrics.csv`、`ranking.json`、`robustness.json` 和 `data/etf_portfolio/weight_calibration/<run_id>/candidate_weight_sets.json/csv`。Search payload 披露 total valid candidate count、evaluated candidate count、baseline weights、benchmark metrics、HistoricalWeightScore components、walk-forward/regime slice metrics、stability score、hard blockers、blocked candidates、market regime、historical range preset 和 requested date range。TRADING-078B 新增 `aits etf weight-calibration export-top --latest --top N` / `--run-id <run_id>`，输出 `reports/etf_portfolio/weight_calibration/top_candidates/top_weight_candidates_<run_id>_topN.json/csv/md`，列出 rank、weight_set_id、weights、historical score、CAGR、max drawdown、Sharpe/Sortino/Calmar、turnover、cash / semiconductor exposure、benchmark excess、drawdown reduction vs QQQ、overfit risk、forward readiness status、blockers、warnings 和 safety fields；blocked candidates 不静默丢弃，而是标记 `blocked_by_risk`、`blocked_by_data_quality` 或 `blocked_by_overfit_risk`。TRADING-078C 新增 `aits etf weight-calibration comparison --latest --top N` / `--run-id <run_id>`，输出 `reports/etf_portfolio/weight_calibration/comparison/candidate_weight_comparison_<run_id>.json/csv/md`，以 deterministic order 展示 current baseline、Buy & Hold QQQ/SPY/SMH、static reference candidates 和 Top-N candidate rows；缺失指标保留 null 并写入 `metric_null_reasons`，仍固定 safety fields。TRADING-078D 新增 `aits etf weight-calibration regime-robustness --latest --top N` / `--run-id <run_id>`，输出 `reports/etf_portfolio/weight_calibration/regime_robustness/regime_robustness_heatmap_<run_id>.json/csv/md`，生成 Top-N candidate x required regime matrix；缺失 regime slice 保留 `MISSING` 与 `REGIME_SLICE_MISSING`，不补造样本或指标。`aits etf weight-calibration register-candidates --run-id/--latest --top N` 把 selected historical candidates 写入 ignored `data/etf_portfolio/weight_calibration/candidate_weight_registry.json`，保留 `weight_set_id`、source search run、rank、weights、metrics summary、robustness summary、blockers、selection reason、config hash、status 和 safety fields；重复登记同一 `weight_set_id` 为 idempotent update。`aits etf weight-calibration enroll-forward --weight-set <id>` 或 `--latest --top N` 只把 safe candidate 登记到 ignored `data/etf_portfolio/weight_calibration/forward_enrollments.json`，生成 `shadow_id`、nested shadow-style record、`forward_tracking_link`、tracking state、historical source linkage、metrics/robustness snapshot 和 safety fields；blocked/rejected/needs_more_data candidates 不能 enroll。`aits etf weight-calibration aggregate-evidence --as-of YYYY-MM-DD` 读取 candidate registry、forward enrollment ledger、optional historical search summary 和 optional forward/weekly/journal/parameter-review JSON，输出 `reports/etf_portfolio/weight_calibration/evidence/backtest_forward_evidence_YYYY-MM-DD.json/md`；每个 record 链接 `weight_set_id`、`shadow_id` 和 source search run，计算 `expectation_gap`、`drawdown_gap`、`turnover_gap`、`stability_gap`，并输出 `consistent`、`forward_better_than_backtest`、`forward_worse_than_backtest`、`mixed`、`blocked` 或 `needs_more_forward_data`。缺少 forward row 或 forward days 不足时必须保持 `needs_more_forward_data`，不得补造 forward conclusion。`aits etf weight-calibration overfit-diagnostics` 读取 candidate registry、optional search summary 和 optional TRADING-071F evidence，输出 `reports/etf_portfolio/weight_calibration/overfit_diagnostics/overfit_diagnostics_*.json/md`；component diagnostics 覆盖 performance concentration、single-period dependency、regime fragility、turnover instability、constraint hit instability、weight extremeness、benchmark dependency 和 forward/backtest divergence，并输出 low/medium/high/critical risk band。`aits etf weight-calibration generate-proposals` 读取 candidate registry、optional TRADING-071F evidence 和 optional TRADING-071G diagnostics，输出 `reports/etf_portfolio/weight_calibration/proposals/candidate_weight_proposals_*.json/md`；proposal types 只允许 `continue_forward_observation`、`reject_weight_set`、`defer_until_more_forward_data`、`propose_extended_shadow` 和 `propose_manual_baseline_review`，并显式阻断 `apply_weight_set`、`promote_to_production`、`enable_broker_action`。`aits etf weight-calibration report --latest` 或显式 artifact paths 生成 `reports/etf_portfolio/weight_calibration/reports/dual_track_calibration_YYYY-MM-DD.json/md`，汇总 search configuration、top historical candidates、walk-forward/regime robustness、overfit diagnostics、forward evidence comparison、candidate registry status、proposal scorecard、manual review package、source report links 和 next steps。`aits etf weight-calibration validate` 输出 `reports/etf_portfolio/weight_calibration/validation/weight_calibration_validation_*.json/md`，校验 config、bounded search、sample workflow modules、Reader Brief/report registry visibility、unsafe proposal blockers、evidence-linked proposals 和 proposal-only safety；失败时 fail closed。`config/report_registry.yaml` 和 Reader Brief/report dashboard 只读暴露 latest `etf_weight_dual_track_calibration_report` 和 validation artifact。该 ledger/report/validation/Reader Brief visibility 是 TRADING-071 weight-calibration forward observation state，不写 shared experiment shadow registry `data/simulation/etf_shadow_candidates.json`，不替换 forward dashboard 的 experiment-backed candidates。所有输出固定 `observe_only=true`、`candidate_only=true`、`production_effect=none`、`broker_action=none`、`manual_review_required=true`，并记录 `production_weights_mutated=false` / `applied_weight_set=null`；candidate weights 只是后续 report/manual review 输入，不写 `target_weights.csv`、不修改 baseline config、不触发 broker action。

TRADING-078E `aits etf weight-calibration overfit-explain --latest --top N` / `--run-id <run_id>` 生成 `reports/etf_portfolio/weight_calibration/overfit_explanations/overfit_explanations_<run_id>.json/md` runtime artifacts。该解释层读取 historical search、optional TRADING-078B top export 和 optional TRADING-071G overfit diagnostics，把 candidate-level risk band 转成 human-readable `top_overfit_reasons`、`supporting_metrics`、`blocking_metrics` 和 `manual_review_note`；它只服务人工复核，不登记 candidate、不 enroll shadow、不写 production weights、不修改 baseline config、不触发 broker action，安全字段固定 `observe_only=true`、`candidate_only=true`、`production_effect=none`、`broker_action=none`、`manual_review_required=true`。

TRADING-078F `aits etf weight-calibration enroll-top --latest --top N` / `--run-id <run_id>` 和 `aits etf weight-calibration enroll --latest --weight-set <weight_set_id>` 从 Top-N export 只选择 `forward_readiness_status=shadow_ready` 且无 blockers 的候选，写入 ignored `data/etf_portfolio/weight_calibration/forward_enrollments.json`。Enrollment record 新增可审计 `enrollment_id`、`shadow_candidate_id`、warnings、`source_links` 和 latest selection `enrollment_results`；source links 可指向 historical search、TRADING-078B top export、TRADING-078C comparison table 或后续 recommendation report。该 workflow 不写 shared experiment shadow registry、不写 production weights、不修改 baseline config、不触发 broker action。

TRADING-078G `aits etf weight-calibration recommendation --latest --top N` / `--run-id <run_id>` 生成 `reports/etf_portfolio/weight_calibration/recommendations/initial_weight_recommendation_<run_id>.json/md` runtime report。该报告汇总 historical search metadata、preset/date range、bounded constraints、Top-N candidates、benchmark comparison、regime robustness、overfit explanation、forward readiness、shadow enrollment recommendation、manual review notes、source artifacts 和 next steps；它只输出 candidate-only recommendation，不运行 enrollment、不写 production weights、不修改 baseline config、不触发 broker action。

TRADING-078H Reader Brief `ETF Initial Weight Candidates` 区块只读 report index 指向的 latest `etf_initial_weight_recommendation_report`。该区块展示 latest preset、top candidate、suggested shadow action、overfit risk、best robustness、blocked candidate count、safety status 和 detail report link；缺失 recommendation report 时显示 `MISSING`，不运行 `weight-calibration recommendation`、search、comparison、regime robustness、overfit explanation 或 enrollment 上游。

TRADING-078I `aits etf weight-calibration usability-validate` 生成 `reports/etf_portfolio/weight_calibration/validation/historical_calibration_usability_validation_*.json/md` runtime validation artifacts。该 gate 使用 deterministic sample pipeline 和 optional payload checks，校验 presets、bounded search、Top-N export、comparison、regime robustness、overfit explanation、shadow enrollment、recommendation report、Reader Brief registry visibility、benchmark comparison、overfit explanation coverage 和固定 safety boundary；unsafe production/broker/manual-review/enrollment mutation 状态必须 fail closed。

TRADING-079 `aits etf weight-calibration diagnostics --include-robust-packs` 生成 `reports/etf_portfolio/weight_calibration/search_diagnostics/historical_weight_search_diagnostics_*.json/md`、`*_stable_shapes.csv` 和 `*_near_shadow.csv` runtime artifacts。该诊断层只回答为什么 historical weight search 没有产生 `shadow_ready` candidate，以及哪些 bounded search pack / preset combination 值得人工复核；它比较 `last_2y`、`last_3y`、`last_5y`、`post_2022_bear`、`ai_cycle_recent` 和 `full_available`，输出 per-preset Top-N、overfit risk distribution、shadow-ready count、cross-preset stable weight shapes、near-shadow gaps、rescue suggestions 和 shadow minimum criteria。稳健搜索包在 `config/etf_portfolio/weight_search.yaml` 中显式定义，半导体 exposure 上限收窄；报告不放宽 gate、不注册 candidate、不 enroll shadow、不写 production weights、不修改 baseline config、不触发 broker action。

ETF no-lookahead artifacts 遵守统一 timing contract：raw market data / feature snapshot / signal / allocation decision 使用同一 `t`，最早 execution date 是 `t` 之后的下一交易日，backtest return date 必须晚于 execution date。`data/simulation/etf_ledger.csv` 中的 `forward_return_*`、`relative_return_vs_*`、`max_drawdown_next_*`、`weight_contribution_*`、portfolio-vs-benchmark 和 `signal_hit_*` 字段属于 delayed evaluation，只能在 `evaluation_only=true` 记录中承载；ETF daily brief 的 decision sections 不得引用这些字段。

## Production / advisory 主链路

| Artifact | 由谁生成 | 上游输入 | 关键字段或内容 | 下游使用 | 是否影响 production | 常见误解 |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| `data/raw/prices_daily.csv` | `aits download-data` / `aits data repair-backtest-inputs --price-only` | FMP 股票/ETF、Cboe VIX；repair 时读取 diagnostics repair plan 或显式 `--symbols` | `ticker`、`symbol`、`date`、OHLCV、`adj_close`、source、updated_at、source_symbol、canonical_symbol | `validate-data`、features、backtest、outcome、shadow backtest input diagnostics | 是，作为主价格缓存 | 不是供应商原始响应；已标准化为本地长表；repair 只补价格历史，不补造 signal snapshot 或 production 参数 |
| `data/raw/prices_marketstack_daily.csv` | `aits download-data` | Marketstack | 第二行情源 OHLCV | `validate-data` reconciliation | 是，作为质量核验输入 | 不覆盖主价格缓存 |
| `data/raw/rates_daily.csv` | `aits download-data` | FRED | `series`、`date`、`value` | macro features、quality gate、risk budget | 是 | `DTWEXBGS` 是广义美元指数代理，不是 ICE DXY |
| `data/raw/download_manifest.csv` | `aits download-data` / `aits data repair-backtest-inputs` | 本次下载或 repair 请求 | provider、endpoint、request params、timestamp、row count、checksum、canonical/source symbol mapping | 数据源审计、质量报告、backtest input diagnostics freshness | 是，作为来源审计 | 不包含 API key 或 token 原文；`BRK.B` 等 source alias 必须写入 request params 供审计 |
| `reports/data_governance/pit_source_manifest/<manifest_id>/pit_source_manifest.json`<br/>`pit_source_manifest.md`、`pit_source_manifest_validation.json/md`、`reader_brief_section.md` | `aits data-sources pit-manifest report` / `aits data-sources pit-manifest validate --latest` | `config/data_sources.yaml`、`data/raw/download_manifest.csv`、source catalog cache paths | `report_type=pit_source_manifest`、policy metadata、safety boundary、source records、retrieval_time、effective_date、revision_risk、`STRONG_PIT|APPROX_PIT|NON_PIT|UNKNOWN`、cache path、checksum、refresh policy、validation policy、grade counts、non-strong source ids、validation issues | `config/report_registry.yaml` 的 `pit_source_manifest`、Reader Brief `PIT Source Manifest` 区块、monthly/manual data governance review | 否，`production_effect=none` | Source-level governance manifest 不刷新数据、不运行评分或回测、不修复全部 PIT 问题；`APPROX_PIT`、`NON_PIT`、`UNKNOWN` 不能被解释为 production-grade PIT 证据；warning 是治理调查项，不是静默豁免 |
| `artifacts/data_refresh_audit/validation/validate_data_*.json`<br/>`reports/data_governance/data_refresh_audit/<audit_id>/data_refresh_audit.json`<br/>`data_refresh_audit.md`、`data_refresh_audit_validation.json/md`、`reader_brief_section.md` | `aits validate-data` 写 validation sidecar；`aits data refresh-audit report --as-of YYYY-MM-DD` / `aits data refresh-audit validate --latest` | raw market/macro cache、`outputs/reports/data_quality_YYYY-MM-DD.md`、latest `artifacts/data_refresh/YYYY-MM-DD/market_data_refresh_summary.json`、price cache checksum/row count、U.S. market calendar | `report_type=data_refresh_audit`、audit records、data type、source、start/end time、as_of、status、checksum、record count、warning/error count、market session skip reason、summary failed/skipped/warning/error counts、next action、validation issues、安全字段 | `config/report_registry.yaml` 的 `data_refresh_audit`、Reader Brief `Data Refresh Audit` 区块、paper-shadow freshness/readiness 人工复核 | 否，`production_effect=none` | Audit trail 只读记录 refresh/validation 证据；缺 validation sidecar 必须 fail closed；`SKIPPED_MARKET_CLOSED` / `SKIPPED_NO_NEW_DATA` 不是 fresh data 证明；报告不刷新数据、不补造 cache、不降低 `aits validate-data` 门禁、不写 official target weights、不触发 broker/order |
| `reports/data_governance/data_source_fallback_policy/<report_id>/data_source_fallback_policy.json`<br/>`data_source_fallback_policy.md`、`data_source_fallback_policy_validation.json/md`、`reader_brief_section.md` | `aits data fallback-policy run --as-of YYYY-MM-DD`、`aits data fallback-policy report --latest`、`aits data fallback-policy validate --latest` | `config/data_source_fallback_policy.yaml`、`config/data_sources.yaml`、显式 `--unavailable-source-id` / `--fallback-used-source-id` / `--fallback-reason` declarations | `report_type=data_source_fallback_policy`、source groups、source priority、source eligibility、fallback states `PRIMARY_OK|FALLBACK_USED|FALLBACK_UNAVAILABLE|BLOCKED_NO_VALID_SOURCE`、fallback metadata、blocking data types、Reader Brief section、validation issues、安全字段 | `config/report_registry.yaml` 的 `data_source_fallback_policy`、Reader Brief `Data Source Fallback Policy` 区块、data refresh audit、PIT source manifest、evidence staleness monitor、shadow continuation readiness | 否，`production_effect=none` | Fallback policy 只定义和披露 source fallback 状态；`FALLBACK_USED` 不是 silent replacement，也不是 production approval；`FALLBACK_UNAVAILABLE` / `BLOCKED_NO_VALID_SOURCE` 必须 fail closed；报告不下载数据、不写 cache、不运行评分/回测、不触发 broker/order |
| `reports/data_governance/cache_catalog/<catalog_id>/cache_catalog.json`<br/>`cache_catalog.md`、`cache_catalog_validation.json/md`、`reader_brief_section.md` | `aits data cache-catalog run --as-of YYYY-MM-DD`、`aits data cache-catalog report --latest`、`aits data cache-catalog validate --latest` | `config/cache_catalog.yaml`、`config/data_sources.yaml`、price / secondary price / macro / market panel cache、latest validation sidecar、latest data refresh audit、可选 explicit expected checksum 或 previous catalog | `report_type=cache_catalog`、policy metadata、safety boundary、cache entry records、artifact id、data type、cache path、as_of、checksum、row/column count、created/modified timestamp、source ids/names、validation timestamp、refresh audit id、missing required entries、checksum mismatch entries、validation issues、安全字段 | `config/report_registry.yaml` 的 `cache_catalog`、Reader Brief `Cache Catalog` 区块、data refresh audit、PIT source manifest、evidence staleness monitor、shadow continuation readiness | 否，`production_effect=none` | Cache catalog 只读扫描既有 cache，不刷新、不修复、不补造缺失 cache；missing required、unreadable cache 或 checksum mismatch 必须 fail closed；latest pointer 不是数据输入；缺 artifact 时下游 summary 显示 `MISSING`，不得补造 cache integrity 结论 |
| `outputs/reports/data_quality_YYYY-MM-DD.md` | `aits validate-data` | raw market/macro cache、download manifest、data quality config | data quality status、schema、freshness、duplicates、suspicious values、reconciliation | features、score-daily、backtest 前置门禁 | 是，失败时下游应停止 | PASS 不等于投资结论可靠，只代表数据缓存可继续用 |

| `outputs/reports/feature_availability_YYYY-MM-DD.md` | `build-features` / `score-daily` / `backtest` | `config/feature_availability.yaml`、feature rows | PIT availability、future rows、fallback 策略 | score-daily、backtest fail-closed | 是 | 缺少 availability rule 不是小问题，会触发 fail closed |
| `data/processed/sec_fundamentals_YYYY-MM-DD.csv` | SEC/TSM fundamentals pipeline | SEC companyfacts、TSMC IR | metric、period、filed/disclosed dates、value | fundamental scoring | 是 | TSM 可由官方 IR 合并，不等同 SEC companyfacts 缺失 |
| `data/processed/sec_features_YYYY-MM-DD.csv` | `aits fundamentals build-sec-features` / `score-daily` | SEC-style metrics | margin、R&D、CapEx 等特征 | fundamental component | 是 | 单位或周期不一致时会跳过或告警，不应手工平滑 |
| `data/raw/sec_edgar/*` + `data/processed/sec_edgar/*.csv` + `outputs/reports/sec_pit_backfill/*` | `aits sec-pit backfill` / `scripts/run_sec_pit_backfill.py` | SEC submissions、SEC companyfacts、fundamental metric/feature policy | raw manifest checksum、filing timeline、fact availability、PIT intervals、daily panel、feature panel、coverage/leakage validation | B-grade reconstructed filing-time fundamentals for backtest/score loaders | 否，`production_effect=none` | 默认是 `B_RECONSTRUCTED_SEC_FILING_PIT`，不是 strict vendor archive；不得只按 fiscal period end 合并 |
| `outputs/sec_pit_evaluation/sec_pit_evaluation_summary_YYYY-MM-DD.json/md` + `sec_pit_feature_effectiveness_YYYY-MM-DD.csv` + `sec_pit_signal_attribution_YYYY-MM-DD.csv` + `sec_pit_shadow_candidate_weights_YYYY-MM-DD.csv` | `aits sec-pit evaluate` / `scripts/run_sec_pit_evaluation.py` | `sec_pit_feature_panel.csv`、SEC company universe 或 `--tickers`、cached prices/rates、`config/sec_pit_evaluation.yaml` | summary JSON/Markdown、feature effectiveness、signal attribution、shadow candidate weights、data quality status、PIT safety、IC/RankIC、top-bottom spread、coverage、stability、PIT quality、recommendation | SEC PIT cognitive evaluation、shadow weight iteration 候选输入；daily task dashboard 只读卡片 | 否，`production_effect=none` | shadow candidate 不是 production 权重晋级；本命令会先跑 `validate_data_cache`；缺少 `available_time` 或 `available_time > decision_time` 的行会被排除并计数；所有 shadow weights 固定 `manual_review_required=true`、`production_effect=none` |
| `outputs/sec_pit_baseline_comparison/sec_pit_baseline_comparison_summary_YYYY-MM-DD.json/md` + `sec_pit_decision_impact_YYYY-MM-DD.csv` + `sec_pit_rank_shift_YYYY-MM-DD.csv` + `sec_pit_incremental_alpha_YYYY-MM-DD.csv` | `aits sec-pit compare-baseline` | TRADING-040 SEC PIT evaluation artifacts、score-daily baseline CSV 或 baseline score CSV | comparison status、baseline artifact path/status/rows/date range、decision impact、rank shift、incremental alpha bucket、top promoted/downgraded ticker、feature drivers、PIT safety、manual review policy、SEC lineage 汇总 | 判断 SEC PIT fundamentals 相对 baseline 是否改善排序、回撤规避和人工复核队列；daily task dashboard 只读卡片；TRADING-042 provenance / label 诊断输入 | 否，`production_effect=none` | 缺 baseline 或 evaluation 默认生成 LIMITED report；默认 `outputs/daily_score` 缺失时可 fallback 到 `data/processed/scores_daily.csv` 并记录 `FALLBACK_USED`；不创建市场数据管线；不修改 production weights/actions；所有 decision impact 固定 `manual_review_required=true`、`production_effect=none` |
| `outputs/sec_pit_diagnostics/sec_pit_real_run_diagnostics_YYYY-MM-DD.json/md` + `sec_pit_provenance_gap_YYYY-MM-DD.csv` + `sec_pit_coverage_audit_YYYY-MM-DD.csv` + `sec_pit_alias_resolution_audit_YYYY-MM-DD.csv` + `sec_pit_label_coverage_audit_YYYY-MM-DD.csv` + `sec_pit_candidate_sensitivity_YYYY-MM-DD.csv` | `aits sec-pit diagnose-run` | SEC PIT feature panel、latest evaluation artifacts、latest baseline comparison artifacts、baseline score artifact、`config/ticker_aliases.yaml` | provenance loss stage、alias audit、baseline artifact status、label coverage、coverage ratio before/after、duplicate observations、near-promotion sensitivity | 判断真实 SEC PIT run 是否足够可信，作为 TRADING-043 前置复核；daily task dashboard 只读卡片 | 否，`production_effect=none` | 诊断命令不重跑 evaluation/comparison、不下载数据、不修改 production 或 shadow weights；candidate sensitivity 只是假设 provenance 修复后的人工复核输入，不是 promotion |
| `outputs/sec_pit_candidate_review/sec_pit_candidate_review_summary_YYYY-MM-DD.json/md` + `sec_pit_candidate_evidence_YYYY-MM-DD.csv` + `sec_pit_candidate_by_ticker_YYYY-MM-DD.csv` + `sec_pit_candidate_by_period_YYYY-MM-DD.csv` + `sec_pit_candidate_overlap_with_baseline_YYYY-MM-DD.csv` + `sec_pit_candidate_shadow_proposal_YYYY-MM-DD.csv` | `aits sec-pit review-candidates` / `scripts/run_sec_pit_candidate_review.py` | TRADING-040 evaluation artifacts、TRADING-041 baseline comparison artifacts、TRADING-042 diagnostics artifacts | review status、candidate evidence、by-ticker concentration、by-period stability、baseline overlap / redundancy risk、observe-only shadow proposal、manual review checklist | 为 `capex_intensity` 等 SEC PIT shadow candidate 生成人工复核 evidence pack；daily task dashboard 只读卡片 | 否，`production_effect=none` | review 不是 promotion；不写 production weights、不写 active shadow weights；缺 baseline fields 时 overlap 降级为 `LIMITED_BASELINE_FIELDS_MISSING`；proposal 只建议人工复核 observe-only shadow iteration |
| `outputs/sec_pit_shadow_observe/sec_pit_shadow_observe_summary_YYYY-MM-DD.json/md` + `sec_pit_shadow_scores_YYYY-MM-DD.csv` + `sec_pit_shadow_rank_shift_YYYY-MM-DD.csv` + `sec_pit_shadow_bucket_comparison_YYYY-MM-DD.csv` + `sec_pit_shadow_monitoring_plan_YYYY-MM-DD.csv` + `sec_pit_shadow_safety_audit_YYYY-MM-DD.csv` | `aits sec-pit shadow-observe` | TRADING-043 candidate review、TRADING-040 evaluation attribution、TRADING-041 baseline comparison、TRADING-042 diagnostics、SEC PIT feature panel、baseline score CSV、`config/sec_pit_shadow_observe.yaml` | observe-only lane metadata、baseline/label coverage ratio、monitoring status reason、factor/data trigger flags、safety audit、`normalized_feature_value * observe_weight` shadow component、observe-only score、rank shift、bucket comparison、monitoring plan、manual review checklist | 隔离观察已人工批准的 SEC PIT candidate 如果进入评分会怎样影响 score/rank；daily task dashboard 只读卡片 | 否，`production_effect=none` | 只支持 observe-only monitoring，不是 production promotion；默认 baseline dir 优先读取 research-only `data/processed/research/scores_daily_backfill_sec_pit_2023_2026.csv`，显式 `--baseline-score-path` 才覆盖；不覆盖 baseline score、不改 production weights、不改 active shadow weights；critical safety check 失败时只写 safety audit 和 degraded summary；baseline/label/sample gate 未通过时输出 `LIMITED_BASELINE_MISSING`、`LIMITED_LABELS_MISSING` 或 `INSUFFICIENT_MONITORING_SAMPLE`，不得误报 `ROLLBACK_TRIGGERED_BY_FACTOR` |
| `outputs/sec_pit_baseline_coverage/sec_pit_baseline_coverage_summary_YYYY-MM-DD.json/md` + `sec_pit_baseline_coverage_by_ticker_YYYY-MM-DD.csv` + `sec_pit_baseline_coverage_by_date_YYYY-MM-DD.csv` + `sec_pit_baseline_gap_YYYY-MM-DD.csv` | `aits sec-pit audit-baseline-coverage` | SEC PIT feature panel、baseline score CSV | expected/actual/missing rows、coverage ratio、score completeness、by-ticker/date coverage、gap type 和 recommended fix | shadow observe 前的数据覆盖审计；daily task dashboard 只读卡片 | 否，`production_effect=none` | 只读审计，不运行 backfill、不运行 shadow-observe、不修改 baseline CSV；`MISSING_BASELINE` / `INSUFFICIENT_COVERAGE` 是数据限制，不是因子失败 |
| `outputs/sec_pit_shadow_monitor/sec_pit_shadow_monitor_summary_YYYY-MM-DD.json/md` + `sec_pit_shadow_rolling_metrics_YYYY-MM-DD.csv` + `sec_pit_shadow_warning_events_YYYY-MM-DD.csv` | `aits sec-pit shadow-monitor` | TRADING-044 shadow observe summary/scores/bucket/monitoring plan、TRADING-045 baseline coverage summary、research-only baseline score CSV | monitor status、monitor maturity、rolling metrics availability、state transition reason、20D/60D rolling RankIC、hit rate、relative return vs baseline、drawdown improvement、semiconductor/platform bucket RankIC、sample count、elapsed/remaining days、warning events、rollback recommendation gate | `capex_intensity` observe-only lane 的持续监控；daily task dashboard 只读卡片 | 否，`production_effect=none` | 不是新因子、不是权重调整、不是 active shadow 更新；coverage gate 通过但 minimum evidence 未达标时输出 `MONITORING_ACTIVE`；coverage/sample/days 达标且无 warning/rollback 时输出 `OK_MONITORING`，rolling metrics 暂缺只阻断 rollback，不再解释为 sample insufficiency；baseline coverage gate 未通过、rolling metrics 不可用或 factor underperformance 未经确认时不得输出 rollback；`ROLLBACK_RECOMMENDED` 仍只表示人工复核建议，不修改 production 或交易行为 |
| `data/external/valuation_snapshots/*.yaml` | `aits valuation fetch-fmp` 或人工导入 | FMP / 可审计估值来源 | valuation percentile、crowding、EPS revision、PIT metadata | valuation component、valuation gate | 是 | 过期或 public convenience 来源不能伪装成高可信生产输入 |
| `data/external/risk_event_occurrences/*.yaml` | 风险事件导入、LLM formal、人工复核 | 官方来源、LLM precheck、review attestation | risk id、level、evidence grade、lifecycle、action class | policy/geopolitics score、risk gate、alerts | 是 | LLM formal 不是人工复核，B 级 evidence 不能单独触发 gate |
| `data/processed/risk_event_prereview_queue.json` | `aits score-daily` OpenAI 预审、`aits risk-events precheck-triaged-official-candidates`、`aits risk-events import-llm-claims` | 官方政策/地缘候选、OpenAI metadata-only 预审、cache metadata、visibility cutoff 审计 | schema version、risk_id、candidate level、llm_extracted / pending_review、model、reasoning effort、request_timestamp、cache status、source URL | 人工风险事件复核、LLM formal assessment 输入、replay cache-only 过滤、预审报告和 dashboard 审计 | 否，待复核队列本身不直接影响评分；人工确认或 LLM formal 写入 occurrence 后才进入 policy/geopolitics score | pending_review 不是已发生风险；晚于可见窗口或缺可证明时间戳的记录不能用于历史 replay 结论 |
| `data/external/trade_theses/*.yaml` | 人工维护 | thesis、验证指标、证伪条件 | status、review state、invalidators | thesis gate、日报解释 | 是，对 active_trade 纪律有效 | watch_only ticker 缺 thesis 不等于 thesis 失败 |
| `data/external/portfolio_positions/current_positions.csv` | 人工持仓快照 | 真实账户持仓 | ticker、市值、AI exposure、节点/地区/因子 | portfolio exposure、risk budget 扩展 | Advisory 输入 | 缺失时不能用观察池或模型建议仓位替代真实持仓 |
| `data/processed/scores_daily.csv` | `aits score-daily` | features、fundamentals、valuation、risk、weights、gates | production row 含 component score、overall、confidence、effective weights、model/final position、gate summary | 日报、snapshot、dashboard、previous comparison、SEC PIT baseline comparison | 是，作为评分输出 | 不等于交易指令，也不等于账户实际仓位；research backfill 默认不得写入该路径，除非额外显式传 `--overwrite-production-path` |
| `data/processed/research/scores_daily_backfill_*.csv` | `aits score-daily backfill-baseline` | 已通过门禁的 market/macro cache 和 existing score-daily logic | research baseline row 至少含 `decision_date`、`ticker`、`baseline_score`、`baseline_rank`、`baseline_action`、score source/version、feature completeness、`research_backfill=true`、`production_effect=none` | SEC PIT shadow baseline coverage、shadow observe research baseline | 否，`production_effect=none` | 这是 historical shadow monitoring baseline，不是 production score cache；默认隔离在 `data/processed/research/`，不写 decision snapshot、prediction ledger 或 order intent |
| `outputs/reports/daily_score_YYYY-MM-DD.md` | `aits score-daily` | scores、quality、features、manual inputs、trace context | Decision Card status、Data Lineage、funnel、gate ladder、module scores、review sections | 人读主报告、dashboard 输入 | Advisory / trend judgment | 报告仓位是解释区间，不是自动买卖 |
| `data/processed/decision_snapshots/decision_snapshot_YYYY-MM-DD.json` | `aits score-daily` | 当日评分上下文、gate、quality、trace | market regime、scores、confidence、positions、position_gates、trace refs | feedback、shadow、replay、dashboard | 是，记录 production 判断 | 不是回测结果，且不应被后验 outcome 改写 |
| `outputs/reports/calculation_explainers_YYYY-MM-DD.json` | `aits score-daily` / `aits reports calculation-explainers` | `data/processed/decision_snapshots/decision_snapshot_YYYY-MM-DD.json`、`config/metric_explainers.yaml`、可选 `data/processed/scores_daily.csv` | `schema_version=1`、`report_type=calculation_explainers`、`production_effect=none`、metric formula、input fields / values、source artifacts、PIT policy、limitations、overall/component/effective weight/confidence/gate/final position explainers；RankIC / max drawdown / baseline coverage 在非回测上下文为 `DEFINITION_ONLY` | Reader Brief 和后续 HTML 解释层的只读输入；当前也可人工审计“这个数字怎么算” | 否，`production_effect=none` | 它不重新计算 score、不修改 weights/gates，也不替代 decision snapshot；缺少 optional scores cache 只进入 warning |
| `outputs/reports/evidence/daily_score_YYYY-MM-DD_trace.json` | `aits score-daily` | report claims、evidence、datasets、quality、run manifest | claim/evidence/dataset/quality refs、run id、rule versions、weight calibration | dashboard、trace lookup、审计 | 不直接改变结果 | 不是日报正文，而是证据索引 |
| `data/processed/prediction_ledger.csv` | `score-daily` / challenger shadow | decision snapshot、trace | candidate_id、production_effect、signal date、score、final position、outcome status | outcome calibration、shadow maturity | production 行影响正式观察；challenger 行必须隔离解释 | 后验 outcome 不应改写 signal-time 输入 |
| `outputs/reports/evidence_dashboard_YYYY-MM-DD.html` | `aits reports dashboard` | daily report、trace、snapshot、belief state、alerts、scores | dashboard status、分层展示结论、evidence、dataset、quality、gate、trend | 本地只读下钻 | 否，`production_effect=none` | dashboard 不替代 Markdown 日报和 trace 的审计责任 |

## Daily-run / replay 运行产物

| Artifact | 由谁生成 | 上游输入 | 关键字段或内容 | 下游使用 | 是否影响 production | 常见误解 |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| `outputs/reports/daily_ops_plan_YYYY-MM-DD.md` | `aits ops daily-plan` / `daily-run` | market calendar、env presence、config | planned commands、required env、expected artifacts、skip reason | 调度前检查、daily-run | 否，只读计划 | 计划报告不代表命令已经执行 |
| `outputs/reports/daily_ops_run_YYYY-MM-DD.md` | `aits ops daily-run` | plan、实际子命令结果 | step status、exit code、duration、artifact paths、失败诊断路径 | 运行审计、问题定位 | 是，作为生产运行审计 | 主报告不保存 stdout/stderr 原文或 secret；失败输出只在独立脱敏诊断 artifact 中保留 |
| `outputs/runs/daily/<executed_at>/as_of_YYYY-MM-DD__<run_id>/reports/diagnostics/daily_ops_step_failure_YYYY-MM-DD_<step>_<timestamp>.md` | `aits ops daily-run` | 失败子命令的 stdout/stderr、return code、env secret presence | 命令、退出码、stdout/stderr 行数、脱敏 stdout/stderr、可选 artifact error | 失败排查、root cause 复核 | 是，作为生产运行审计 | 仅失败步骤生成；API key/token/Authorization 和敏感 env 值必须脱敏；不是供应商付费内容归档 |
| `outputs/reports/daily_task_dashboard_YYYY-MM-DD.html/json` | `aits ops daily-run` / `aits reports daily-tasks` | daily_ops_run metadata、本轮同日子报告、evidence dashboard JSON、最近可用 shadow parameter search bundle、最近同日 `shadow_iteration_YYYY-MM-DD.json`、可选同日 `paper_trading_summary_YYYY-MM-DD.json`、可选同日 `paper_signal_quality_YYYY-MM-DD.json`、可选同日 `shadow_parameter_impact_YYYY-MM-DD.json`、可选同日
