`daily_weight_adjustment_summary_YYYY-MM-DD.json`、可选同日 `research_governance_summary_YYYY-MM-DD.json`、可选 shadow weight iteration current/candidate JSON、可选 shadow vs production comparison JSON、最近 7/14/30 日已存在的 paper trading summary 和 order intent candidate JSON、可选最近已有 `paper_trading_replay_START_END.json`、search window 内 production decision snapshots | `key_conclusions`、投资动作/仓位/置信度/Data Gate、数据可信度、参数治理、反馈复盘、shadow parameter 诊断领先 trial 与收益差距、Shadow Iteration Status 只读卡片、Paper Trading Summary（candidate_count、blocked_candidates、generated_intents、approved/rejected、submitted、filled/open、reconciliation_status）、Paper Trading Trend（7/14/30 日窗口、latest `replay_mode` / `portfolio_carry_forward`、summary 可用/缺失、候选/订单/成交/PnL/reconciliation、synthetic snapshot 使用比例、top `blocked_by`、top `reason_code`；最近 replay 为 `continuous_portfolio` 时额外展示 final_equity、max_drawdown、exposure_peak、final_positions count 和 expired DAY orders）、Paper Signal Quality 轻量卡片（evaluation_status、主要 `blocked_by`、synthetic_snapshot_ratio、sample_count、report link、observe-only / `production_effect=none`）、Shadow Impact 轻量卡片（impact_status、主要 blocked_by / warnings、7/14/30 日 production/shadow/unknown 样本数、production vs shadow filled_count、paper PnL、continuous replay availability/mode、report link）、Weight Adjustment Candidate 轻量卡片（candidate_count、top_candidate_id、gate_status、main blocked_by、report link、`production_effect=none`）、Weight Candidate Evaluation 轻量卡片（evaluation_status、candidate_count、evaluable_candidate_count、top_candidate_id、main blocked_by、report link、`production_effect=none`）、Weight Promotion Gate 轻量卡片（gate_status、candidate_count、ready_for_manual_review_count、blocked_count、top_candidate_id、main blocked_by、report link、`production_effect=none`）、Daily Weight Adjustment Summary 轻量卡片（candidate_count、evaluation_status、promotion_gate_status、ready_for_manual_review_count、main blocked_by、report link、`production_effect=none`、manual_review_only）、Research Governance Summary 轻量卡片（card_count、missing/limited/warning counts、manual_review_required_count、group_counts、report link、`production_effect=none`）、Shadow Weight Iteration 轻量卡片（current weights、latest decision、latest delta、candidate report link、`production_effect=none`、manual_review_only）、Shadow vs Production Comparison 轻量卡片（status、production decision、shadow decision、score_delta、decision_changed、main reason、report link、`production_effect=none`、manual_review_only）、production/current vs shadow candidate 结果对比表（Total return、Max drawdown、Turnover、Beat rate、样本覆盖和 return 计算口径）、分区参数对比表（Gate cap override 与权重参数，含 production 实际 gate cap 数值/区间）、运行健康、任务状态、子报告 `href` 和可点击子任务下钻入口 | 每日关键结论入口 | 否，`production_effect=none` | 任务状态是审计信息，不是页面首要结论；dashboard 不重新计算 shadow iteration、shadow impact、weight adjustment candidates、weight candidate evaluation、weight promotion gate、daily weight adjustment summary、research governance summary、shadow weight iteration 或 shadow vs production comparison，也不触发 paper trading、paper replay、真实 broker、参数晋级或调参应用，只读取 JSON；dashboard 的 Shadow Impact、Weight Adjustment Candidate、Weight Candidate Evaluation、Weight Promotion Gate、Daily Weight Adjustment Summary、Research Governance Summary、Shadow Weight Iteration 和 Shadow vs Production Comparison 都只展示轻量摘要，不展示 JSON/Markdown 长表；shadow parameter 诊断领先、Shadow Impact、Weight Adjustment Candidate、Weight Candidate Evaluation、Weight Promotion Gate、Daily Weight Adjustment Summary、Research Governance Summary、Shadow Weight Iteration 和 Shadow vs Production Comparison 均不等于可上线；Paper Trading Summary / Trend / Signal Quality / Shadow Impact / Weight Adjustment Candidate / Weight Candidate Evaluation / Weight Promotion Gate / Daily Weight Adjustment Summary / Research Governance Summary / Shadow Weight Iteration / Shadow vs Production Comparison 只展示模拟执行复盘和只读质量解释，缺历史 summary、candidate JSON、continuous replay、signal quality JSON、shadow impact JSON、weight adjustment candidate JSON、weight candidate evaluation JSON、weight promotion gate JSON、daily weight adjustment summary JSON、research governance summary JSON、shadow weight iteration JSON 或 shadow vs production comparison JSON 显示 `LIMITED` / `MISSING` / `INSUFFICIENT_DATA` 或 `continuous_replay_missing` warning 且不补造结论，`LIMITED` / `ERROR` 不阻断主报告；daily-independent 趋势或 replay 不是连续组合收益，continuous replay 摘要也不是实盘收益或上线依据，paper PnL、shadow current weights 和 comparison score_delta 不改变 production 仓位建议；各子任务 Markdown/HTML/JSON 仍是审计源，后续可升级为专属网页 |

| `outputs/reports/research_roadmap_dashboard_YYYY-MM-DD.json/md`<br/>`outputs/reports/research_roadmap_dashboard_validation_YYYY-MM-DD.json/md` | `aits reports research-roadmap-dashboard --as-of YYYY-MM-DD` / `aits reports validate-research-roadmap-dashboard --latest` | 同日 `outputs/reports/report_index_YYYY-MM-DD.json`；`docs/task_register.md`、`docs/task_register_completed.md`；latest monthly review pack、promotion board、extended shadow protocol、candidate rejection postmortem template、research safety boundary audit、artifact lineage graph、task register consistency | `schema_version=1`、`report_type=research_roadmap_dashboard` / `research_roadmap_dashboard_validation`、`dashboard_status=ROADMAP_HEALTHY|ROADMAP_WARNINGS|ROADMAP_BLOCKED`（validator 兼容 legacy `ROADMAP_WITH_WARNINGS`）、active/completed task summary、open blockers、stale/missing artifacts、active candidates、latest paper-shadow/data-governance/safety/lineage statuses、next recommended tasks、Reader Brief section、safety boundary、`production_effect=none` | report index、Reader Brief Research Roadmap Dashboard 摘要、manual roadmap review、governance end-to-end pack | 否，`production_effect=none` | Dashboard 只读聚合 task registers、report index 和既有 governance artifacts；next recommended tasks 只是 owner/developer review 队列，不自动调度、不修改 task/candidate/paper-shadow 状态、不运行上游、不刷新数据、不补造 artifact、不写 official target weights、不触发 broker/order；缺 source、stale artifact、blocked monthly review、promotion board hold、extended shadow blocked/not ready、safety/lineage blocker 必须可见披露 |

| `outputs/runs/daily/<executed_at>/as_of_YYYY-MM-DD__<run_id>/manifest.json` | `aits ops daily-run` | 本轮 daily-run artifacts | run id、checksum、legacy mirror、visibility cutoff；artifact 记录由 `ArtifactRef` 统一生成 | 复现、归档、审计 | 是，作为运行 bundle | `data/raw` / `data/processed` 仍是状态缓存，不会每轮完整复制；manifest 只记录产物引用和 checksum，不保存 stdout/stderr 原文 |
| `outputs/replays/YYYY-MM-DD/<run_id>/replay_run.md/json` | `aits ops replay-day` | cache-only input freeze | visible cutoff、input blockers、excluded future PIT/valuation/manual/OpenAI inputs、replay artifacts；OpenAI cache-only report 缺失时 queue 先过滤并写入 `source_report_status=MISSING`，再 fail closed | 历史复现、diff、窗口 failure summary source | 否，不改 production artifacts | replay 不是 live daily-run，也不应调用 live provider；report 缺失不能让未来 OpenAI queue 原样进入 replay |
| `outputs/replays/windows/<run_id>/replay_window.md/json` | `aits ops replay-window` | 单日 replay bundle、交易日历 | day_runs status、bundle/report paths、diff status、skipped_dates、失败日 `failure_summary.errors`、`failed_step` 和 blocker artifacts | 窗口级复现验收、归档输入缺口审计 | 否，不改 production artifacts | 窗口整体 FAIL 可能来自少数归档输入缺口；必须看 `failure_summary` 判断是数据缺档、步骤失败还是周末跳过 |
| `outputs/replays/YYYY-MM-DD/<run_id>/input/config/expected_price_tickers.csv` | `replay-day --full-universe` | `config/universe.yaml`、replay 过滤后的 `prices_daily.csv` | ticker、included/excluded status、required_scope、visible_in_replay_price_cache、reason；同一记录登记到 `input_freeze_manifest.csv/json` | replay-scoped `score-daily --expected-price-tickers-path` 数据质量门禁 | 否，不改 production artifacts | 只冻结本次 replay expected ticker 集合；baseline/core/benchmark 缺价格仍 fail closed，full-universe 扩展 ticker 缺 replay 可见价格只进入 exclusion audit；不得补造价格或放宽 production `--full-universe` 校验 |
| `outputs/replays/YYYY-MM-DD/<run_id>/diff_vs_production.md` | `replay-day --compare-to-production` | replay bundle、production artifacts | checksum、row count、status diff | PIT 复核 | 否 | diff 说明产物不同，不自动说明哪个结论正确 |

## Trading engine / paper trading 产物

| Artifact | 由谁生成 | 上游输入 | 关键字段或内容 | 下游使用 | 是否影响 production | 常见误解 |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| `data/trading_engine/audit/{order_intent_log,risk_check_log,order_log,execution_report_log,fill_log,portfolio_snapshot}/YYYY-MM-DD.jsonl` | `ExecutionService` / `JsonlAuditLogger` | paper-only `OrderIntent`、risk result、paper order、execution report、portfolio snapshot | 每行包含 timestamp、run_id、strategy_id、schema_version、source_object_id、payload、`intent_id` 或 `related_intent_ids`；`replay_intent_audit_trace` 可按 intent 回放完整轨迹 | paper trading 审计和测试复现 | 否，paper trading MVP；真实交易仍未启用 | `execution_report_log` 和 `fill_log` 不等价；rejected intent 不应有 broker order 或 fill；portfolio snapshot 可通过 `related_intent_ids` 关联到 intent |
| `reports/trading_daily/YYYY-MM-DD.md` | `scripts/run_paper_trading_demo.py` / `scripts/run_paper_trading_from_candidates.py` / trading report writer | paper trading audit state、orders、fills、portfolio snapshot、ReconciliationResult | OrderIntent 数量、风控通过/拒绝、paper order、成交/未成交/取消、portfolio、realized/unrealized PnL、reconciliation status、`production_effect=none` | paper trading 执行复盘 | 否，`production_effect=none` | 不是实盘交易日报，不代表真实账户、券商状态或真实成交；reconciliation `PASS` 只说明 paper portfolio 与本地 audit/fill 重建一致 |
| `outputs/reports/paper_trading_summary_YYYY-MM-DD.json` | `scripts/run_paper_trading_from_candidates.py` / trading report writer | `order_intent_candidates_YYYY-MM-DD.json`、paper trading report、audit log、ReconciliationResult、可选 historical OHLC | status、candidate_count、blocked_candidates、generated_intents、approved/rejected、submitted、filled/open/cancelled、realized/unrealized PnL、reconciliation_status、market_snapshot_source / counts、audit_log_path、trading daily report path、`production_effect=none` | daily task dashboard 的 Paper Trading Summary 区块和 paper replay 汇总 | 否，`production_effect=none` | 该 JSON 只把模拟执行复盘带回每日主入口；market snapshot 优先 historical OHLC，其次 candidate metadata，最后才 synthetic limit price；`LIMITED` / `ERROR` 不阻断主报告，不代表实盘订单、账户状态或 broker 回报，也不会改变 production 仓位建议 |
| `outputs/reports/paper_trading_replay_START_END.json/md` | `scripts/run_paper_trading_replay.py --start YYYY-MM-DD --end YYYY-MM-DD --mode daily-independent` 或 `--mode continuous-portfolio` | 每日 `order_intent_candidates_YYYY-MM-DD.json`；缺失时由 candidate runner 生成 limited `daily_decision_summary` 和 `order_intent_candidates`；逐日 paper summary / trading daily report / audit log；可选 historical OHLC | `replay_mode`、`portfolio_carry_forward`、`production_effect=none`、`order_expiration_policy`、`unsupported_order_policy`、`continuous_metrics_available`、quality_flags、market_snapshot_source 分布、窗口状态、paper-only execution boundary、candidate / blocked / intent / risk / order / fill / PnL totals、reconciliation_status 分布、按 symbol / strategy_id / reason_code / blocked_by 聚合、每日结果和 limited upstream 标记；continuous 额外输出 `expired_day_orders`、`rejected_gtc_orders`、`carried_positions_count`、`final_cash`、`final_equity`、`final_positions`、`max_position_concentration`、`max_drawdown_pct`、equity curve、exposure peak 和 final portfolio summary | paper trading daily flow validation、复盘、dashboard latest replay 摘要和 paper signal quality 可选输入 | 否，`production_effect=none` | `daily-independent` 每天重新初始化组合，不是连续组合收益；`continuous-portfolio` 是 paper-only 连续组合模拟，不是真实账户收益、真实 broker 成交、完整税费/滑点模拟或实盘上线依据；DAY order 当日未成交即过期；GTC / non-DAY candidate 直接 rejected；replay 不读取 broker API key、不调用真实 broker；缺候选只生成 limited artifacts，不补造投资结论 |
| `outputs/reports/paper_signal_quality_YYYY-MM-DD.json/md` | `python scripts/run_paper_signal_quality.py --date YYYY-MM-DD` | 最近 7/14/30 日 `paper_trading_summary_YYYY-MM-DD.json`、`order_intent_candidates_YYYY-MM-DD.json`、`config/paper_signal_quality_policy.yaml`、可选既有 `paper_trading_replay_START_END.json` | 顶层 `policy_id`、`policy_version`、thresholds snapshot、`evaluation_status`、`evaluation_gate` checks / `blocked_by` / human-readable explanation / reason explanations、`PAPER_ONLY_SIMULATION` warning、daily-independent / no carry-forward 时的 `DAILY_INDEPENDENT_ONLY` warning、sample_count、candidate_count、generated_intents、filled_count、synthetic_snapshot_ratio、historical_ohlc_coverage、reconciliation_pass_ratio、按 strategy_id / symbol / reason_code / blocked_by / confidence bucket / market_snapshot_source 聚合的 sample_count、candidate_count、generated_intents、filled_count、avg_paper_pnl、synthetic_snapshot_ratio、quality_status、observe-only 安全边界、`production_effect=none` | daily task dashboard 的 Paper Signal Quality 轻量卡片、paper signal 质量复核 | 否，`production_effect=none` | 使用 `continuous-portfolio` replay 时不再输出 `DAILY_INDEPENDENT_ONLY`，但仍必须输出 `PAPER_ONLY_SIMULATION`；`evaluation_status` / `quality_status` 只允许 `INSUFFICIENT_DATA`、`OBSERVE_ONLY`、`PROMISING_BUT_LIMITED`、`LOW_DATA_QUALITY`、`UNRELIABLE`，禁止 live/trade/promotion/approval 语义；evaluation gate 只解释 paper signal quality，不影响 production 仓位建议、参数晋级、真实交易或 replay；脚本不读取 broker API key、不调用真实 broker、不触发 paper runner/replay；paper PnL 只作诊断字段，不是上线依据 |
| `outputs/reports/shadow_parameter_impact_YYYY-MM-DD.json/md` | `python scripts/run_shadow_parameter_impact.py --date YYYY-MM-DD` | 最近 7/14/30 日 `order_intent_candidates_YYYY-MM-DD.json`、`paper_trading_summary_YYYY-MM-DD.json`、`paper_signal_quality_YYYY-MM-DD.json`、`config/shadow_parameter_impact_policy.yaml`、可选既有 `paper_trading_replay_START_END.json` | `impact_status`（仅 `INSUFFICIENT_DATA` / `OBSERVE_ONLY` / `SHADOW_PROMISING_BUT_LIMITED` / `NO_CLEAR_IMPROVEMENT` / `SHADOW_UNRELIABLE` / `LOW_DATA_QUALITY`）、`policy_id`、`policy_version`、`thresholds_snapshot`、`impact_gate` checks / blocked_by / warnings / explanation / reason explanations、production / shadow / unknown source_profile 分类、candidate_count、generated_intents、approved/rejected、submitted/filled/open/cancelled、realized/unrealized paper PnL、synthetic_snapshot_ratio、historical_ohlc_coverage、reconciliation_pass_ratio、blocked_by / reason_code / confidence bucket performance、continuous replay availability、source artifact path / mode / date range、profile final_equity / max_drawdown（仅 continuous portfolio 可用时）、observe-only 安全边界、`production_effect=none` | daily task dashboard 的 Shadow Impact 轻量卡片、shadow 参数 paper/replay/signal quality 复核 | 否，`production_effect=none` | `SHADOW_PROMISING_BUT_LIMITED` 仍不是上线、实盘、交易或参数批准；短期 paper PnL 为正不能单独证明 shadow 更好；缺 shadow 样本、production baseline 或 continuous replay 时输出 `continuous_replay_missing` warning；daily-independent replay 不会被当作 continuous portfolio 结果；synthetic snapshot 或 OHLC 覆盖问题会输出 `LOW_DATA_QUALITY` 或 gate blocked；脚本不读取 broker API key、不调用真实 broker、不触发 paper runner/replay、不改变 production 参数、仓位建议、参数晋级或交易执行 |

## Backtest / feedback 产物

| Artifact | 由谁生成 | 上游输入 | 关键字段或内容 | 下游使用 | 是否影响 production | 常见误解 |

| `outputs/backtests/backtest_daily_YYYY-MM-DD_YYYY-MM-DD.csv` | `aits backtest` | daily scoring context | signal date、score、target exposure、next return、costs、gates | robustness、gate attribution、parameter replay | 否 | 不是 production ledger |
| `outputs/backtests/backtest_robustness_YYYY-MM-DD.json/md` | `aits backtest --robustness-report` | 已完成的 backtest daily rows、robustness / validation policy、benchmark and cost assumptions | `schema_version`、robustness scenario status、coverage/source veto、OOS / random / signal-family baseline evidence、drawdown / turnover / bootstrap evidence、`production_effect=none` | parameter replay、research governance summary、manual promotion review | 否，`production_effect=none` | robustness 证据不是 production approval；scenario leading 或 robustness PASS 仍需 owner review、forward shadow 和 promotion contract，不自动改 scoring rules、weights 或 position gates |
| `outputs/backtests/backtest_input_coverage_*.csv` | `aits backtest` | PIT slices、quality reports | source coverage、missing inputs、warning status | audit、candidate veto | 否 | 高收益但覆盖不足不应直接晋级 |
| `outputs/reports/parameter_replay_YYYY-MM-DD.md/json` | `aits feedback build-parameter-replay` | robustness summary | scenario deltas、materiality、limitations | parameter candidate ledger | 否 | as-if replay 不是 approved overlay |
| `data/processed/parameter_candidates.json` | `aits feedback build-parameter-candidates` | parameter replay | candidate id、trial metrics、veto reasons、governance status | parameter governance、shadow runner | 否 | candidate ready 不等于 owner approval |

| `data/processed/shadow_iteration_registry.csv` + `outputs/reports/shadow_iteration_YYYY-MM-DD.md/json` + `outputs/shadow_iterations/<run_id>/*` | `aits feedback run-shadow-iteration` / `aits feedback register-forward-shadow` | search bundle、promotion contract、既有 registry | `weight_only` / `gate_only` / `weight_gate_bundle` 分类、lifecycle status、Trial Card、blocked reasons、retirement evidence、P2 guardrails、attribution、position change 降级状态、lineage | dashboard 只读展示、forward shadow 候选管理 | 否，`production_effect=none` | iteration registry 只管理 shadow 观察状态；`register-forward-shadow` 只改 registry 状态；`gate_only` 和 bundle 不得被当作权重晋级候选 |
| `data/processed/prediction_ledger_flow_validation.csv` | `aits feedback run-parameter-shadow` | parameter candidates、production snapshot | validation-only challenger predictions | flow validation outcomes | 否 | 不应和正式 `prediction_ledger.csv` 混同 |

## production_effect 标签

| 标签 | 含义 | 典型位置 |
|---|---|---|
| `production` | 正式生产判断链路的一部分，会进入 canonical scoring / snapshot / ledger 语义 | production decision snapshot、production prediction ledger 行 |
| `advisory` | 投研辅助或趋势判断输出，不自动交易 | daily score report、execution advisory |
| `none` | 只读、诊断、shadow 或 validation-only，不改变生产评分、仓位 gate、正式 ledger 或 approved overlay | dashboard、shadow search、flow validation ledger |
| `validation-only` | 用于验证参数、规则或流程，不可当成生产候选批准 | parameter search、shadow gate / weight profiles |
| `blocked` | 被质量、治理、样本、owner approval 或 promotion contract 阻断 | promotion report、candidate governance |

运行时核心标签由 `ai_trading_system.core.production_effect.ProductionEffect` 表达。历史报告中较长的解释性 production effect 文本需要逐处确认语义后再迁移，不能自动归并。

当一个产物声明 `production_effect=none` 时，它仍然可以非常有价值，但价值是诊断、学习、复核或准备 forward shadow，而不是直接改变 production 结论。

## TRADING-219～223 Paper Shadow Selection Drilldown

| 产物 / 文件 | 生成命令 | 输入 | 关键字段 | 消费方 | 改变生产？ | 注意事项 |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| `reports/etf_portfolio/dynamic_v3_rescue/selection_attribution/<attribution_id>/selection_attribution_manifest.json`<br/>`reports/etf_portfolio/dynamic_v3_rescue/limited_long_risk/<risk_review_id>/limited_long_risk_manifest.json`<br/>`reports/etf_portfolio/dynamic_v3_rescue/limited_consistency/<consistency_id>/limited_consistency_manifest.json`<br/>`reports/etf_portfolio/dynamic_v3_rescue/data_warning_impact/<impact_id>/data_warning_impact_manifest.json`<br/>`reports/etf_portfolio/dynamic_v3_rescue/research_method_hardening/<hardening_id>/research_method_hardening_manifest.json` | `aits etf dynamic-v3-rescue selection-attribution run/report`、`limited-long-risk run/report`、`limited-consistency run/report`、`data-warning-impact run/report`、`research-method-hardening run/report` ## TRADING-251～255 Smoothed Method Evidence Drilldown And Forward Confirmation

|Artifact|生成命令|上游输入|关键字段 / schema|下游|Production effect|常见误解|
